Current Affairs Commentary

What is the Truth About the Ceasefire Negotiations in North China? - Zi

Analyzing important current events, so that readers can gain a more accurate understanding of them, in order to curb rampant rumors - this is one of the main missions of newspaper commentary. However, the analysis of events relies on appropriate information. The term "appropriate" includes conditions such as not violating the truth and having reliable sources. Therefore, when a major event occurs in a country, it is necessary for the authorities to provide news reporters with the convenience of gathering news and transmitting information.

The ceasefire negotiations in North China, after a period of serious setbacks, on the morning of the 23rd, the two sides were able to approach each other. For the past week, the progress seemed to be quite smooth. According to foreign dispatches, the first step has already come to an end. However, at this time, because the domestic news media cannot obtain the convenience of gathering and publishing news, there is no way to contribute information that clarifies the truth and benefits understanding to society, let alone base analysis on true events. This allows the opposing side to take the opportunity to implement news policies and spread all kinds of incorrect information. At the same time, the public is unable to fully understand the truth of the negotiations, leading to all kinds of strange rumors and speculations. Under these circumstances, strong individuals are stimulated and indignant, while weak individuals are dispirited by disappointment. If this situation cannot be changed, the impact will be very worrying. The authorities have already announced to the nation the policy of "resisting while negotiating" to deal with the national crisis. Now that negotiations are underway after resistance, it is even more important to disclose all information about the negotiations without concealment, so that the people can understand and seek their sympathy, and not allow themselves to be misled by the opposing side's propaganda and popular rumors, and fall into a state of indignation and discouragement.

That a ceasefire has been reached between the two sides and that the Chinese and Japanese troops are gradually withdrawing backwards - this is an obvious fact. Under this obvious fact, the key points of the understanding between the two sides and the limits of the troop withdrawal are what the people want to know. Since the initial negotiations, Japanese news agencies and newspapers have been spreading rumors that are sufficient to stimulate the Chinese people's psychology, saying what the conditions of understanding are and to which area and location the Chinese army should withdraw. We regard this kind of malicious propaganda news from the opposing side as having very little credible value and do not want to repeat it. It should be noted that all the rumors that have spread in society have originated from the Japanese side's publicity. Now, if we want to effectively prove that the news spread by the Japanese is contrary to the truth and eradicate popular rumors, the fundamental method is to provide the Chinese news media with the convenience of gathering and transmitting news, without the slightest concealment, so that they can reveal the truth and make appropriate analysis.

When a country wants to resolve major events, the sympathy and understanding of the people are necessary conditions. If these conditions cannot be met, things that are beneficial to the country cannot obtain the assistance of the whole country and are difficult to achieve. Responsible authorities, no matter how hard they work, people will not know, and they will inevitably face obstacles. Those who are handling the ceasefire negotiations today must also be deeply aware of this principle. And to seek the sympathy and understanding of the people, open diplomacy is the most appropriate method.

A few years ago, a friend who studied in Germany wrote in a letter praising the German authorities' ingenious method of resolving the anti-Yang Plan tide among the German people after accepting the Young Plan. The method was to use newspapers to convey to the German people the truth about the negotiation process and the difficulties faced by the authorities, and ultimately to seek the people's sympathy and understanding. The tide of opposition soon subsided. We hope that those who are handling the ceasefire negotiations today will use this method that has been proven effective by the German authorities.

After the US Officially Abolished the Gold Standard

Commodity and Securities Market Prices Skyrocket

Financial Circles Talk Extensively About Inflation

(Washington) Today, the Banking and Currency Committees of both the Senate and the House of Representatives passed Steagall's proposal to formally declare the abolition of the gold standard in the United States. (Reuters, 27th)

(New York) The news that the government intends to legislate to abolish the gold standard has sparked a frenzy of skyrocketing commodity and securities market prices. This morning, there were extremely many transactions, and prices surged, which has not been seen for a long time. Important stocks rose by one to six dollars in record-breaking trading, while the dollar depreciated sharply when measured in foreign currencies. The operating tools of the stock exchange were struggling to cope. In the two hours of business on Saturday morning, 4.3 million shares were traded. Many lots involved 5,000 to 25,000 shares. This new mania is clearly a direct result of the government's proposal to abolish the gold clause in public and private contracts. However, some claim that the government's move is just a step to legalize the existing situation. Government bonds are easing, but secondary bonds are very active. Foreign bonds are firm. The bill to abolish the gold standard and the announcement of the Federal Reserve's credit expansion program (i.e., purchasing government bonds in the open market) made Wall Street very busy this morning. Financial circles are full of talk about inflation. There is much discussion about the possibility of establishing an open gold market in New York, imitating London's method. Gold mining companies are naturally welcome, as they can obtain the true value of their gold. Under the current system, gold mining companies must sell their gold at the statutory price of $20.67 per ounce to the Treasury. Gold cannot be freely exported. The mine owners are bound by this method and cannot obtain the gold surplus resulting from the devaluation of the dollar. Although the United Kingdom has abandoned the gold standard, London has a free gold market where the highest selling price can be obtained. Therefore, the value of gold coming in and out of the London gold market every week is in the millions of pounds, as the United Kingdom currently has no restrictions on gold exports. Commodity market prices also rose today, especially in the wheat market. (Reuters, 27th)

(Washington) President Roosevelt has approved the Securities Act, which stipulates that the public must be informed of the details of various securities. In the future, the issuance of new securities will be subject to strict supervision by state authorities. (Reuters, 27th)

(Washington) President Roosevelt has ordered the Postal Savings Bank Management Committee to purchase 100 million yuan of government bonds. This is part of the process of expanding credit through open market operations. (Reuters, 27th)

Germany's Gold Standard Shaken

(Berlin) German officials are paying close attention to the news that the United States has legislated to abolish the gold standard. A spokesman for the German National Bank today discussed the impact of this move on Germany and the question of whether Germany can maintain the gold standard. He said that he was unable to comment on this situation related to Germany, but if the dollar were to be significantly devalued, the important question of whether Germany could maintain the gold standard would arise. (Reuters, 27th)

This Year's

National Ordinary Income Budget

(Nanjing) The estimated national ordinary income for this year, from July 1st to June 30th of next year, is 629,807,622 yuan. All salt tax, customs duties, stamp duties, tobacco and alcohol tax, mining tax, consolidated tax, bank tax, exchange tax, as well as national enterprise income, business income, and various administrative income are included. The previous year's was 678,221,666 yuan. This year's is 48,414,044 yuan less than the previous year's. This is the impact of the occupation of the four northeastern provinces. A. Salt Tax: This year's estimate is 146,748,148 yuan. The previous year's estimate was 164,615,204 yuan. In comparison, this year's is 17,867,056 yuan less than the previous year's. B. Customs Duties: This year's estimate is 330,923,000 yuan. The previous year's was 359,723,741 yuan. In comparison, this year's is 28,800,741 yuan less than the previous year's. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

Jiang Orders Liu and Deng to Cease Fire

Those Who Do Not Obey Central Government Orders Will Be Punished

A dispatch from Hankou states that since capturing Chongning, Liu Wenhui, the commander of the 24th Army, has occupied the south bank of the Pi River. He originally planned to take advantage of the victory to cross the river and advance north, but the 28th Army, led by Deng Xihou, defended the river firmly, and the 29th Army, led by Tian Songyao, arrived to reinforce them, making it difficult to fight one against two. He changed his plan and launched a fierce attack on Huaizhou with three divisions and appointed Chen Hongwen as the commander-in-chief of the attack on Huaizhou. On the 14th, the attack began. The center of the battle shifted to the Chongguan line downstream of the Pi River, and the situation in the upstream became quiet. The garrison commander of Huaizhou was Chen Shunong, the division commander of Deng's army. He came into contact with Liu's army that day. Tian Songyao originally sent two divisions led by Huang Futang and Zeng Nanfu to Deyang and Shifang to assume upstream defense duties. He sent another two brigades of the Dong Zongheng Division to aid Huaizhou, stationed at Zhao Jia Ferry near Huaizhou, as an outpost of Deng's army, and engaged in fierce fighting with the 24th Army. At this point, Tian's army formally joined the whirlpool. Li Qixiang and Luo Zezhou, two units, had previously been ordered by Liu Xiang to concentrate in Lezhi and Yangxian in preparation for armed suppression. Li and Luo sympathized with Deng and would join forces with Deng's troops to attack Jianyang. Once launched, the situation would change again. In addition to ordering Li and Luo to take advantage of opportunities, Liu Xiang's direct line troops, such as Pan Wenhua and Fan Shaozeng's units, had indeed secretly advanced towards Jianjia. It is heard that Jianwei has already entered the Chongqing military range. If they go deeper into Jiading, Liu Wenhui's capture of Huaizhou in one fell swoop would not be enough to compensate for his loss. Liu Xiang would gain without fighting. Liu had previously sent a telegram to persuade both sides to cease hostilities. He has now received replies from Liu and Deng, mutually passing responsibility for the war. Liu Wenhui's telegram briefly stated, "Since leaving the province in Jinkang, the distance has been shocking. Mutual stimulation and collision have led to the current situation of disputes. As for the actions of the Jin troops, like an arrow on a string, there is no way to avoid it. I only hope that the situation does not spread. Now, I am only acting in self-defense and have ordered my subordinates to adhere to your wishes and not to go too far." Deng Lei briefly stated, "Xihou was ordered to suppress bandits this time and was drawing forces from Xindu. He unexpectedly attacked Wenjian with heavy troops and forcibly occupied various organs in the province. He sent 30 to 40 regiments to attack my Fan, Xin, Chong, and Guan counties. Xihou had no choice but to make a legitimate defense and did not cross the defense line by one step, but Liu's troops continued to attack without stopping. I cannot understand his purpose in fighting. I request that he be sanctioned by force so that the ferocious and stubborn know to be vigilant." Both sides have no thorough understanding of ceasing hostilities and making peace, which shows the stubbornness of the Sichuan warlords. They will not stop until both sides are injured. Chiang Kai-shek, the commander-in-chief of bandit suppression stationed in Jiangxi, was deeply saddened to hear that the Sichuan war had expanded. He repeatedly telegraphed both sides to strictly stop it. Recently, he summoned representatives of the Sichuan army in Nanchang and gave instructions, saying, "The national crisis is becoming more urgent, and the Red bandits have not been eliminated. I hope that the generals of the Sichuan army will preserve some personality for the country and avoid being despised by the world. In addition to ordering Liu and Deng to return to their original defenses and wait for a solution, each representative should telegraph their respective armies to immediately cease hostilities. Regardless of which army occupies the other's defense line, the Central Government will order them to return. If they do not comply, they will be punished." After the representatives received the instructions, they telegraphed their respective armies, urging them to cease hostilities. Can the Sichuan warlords stop before it is too late after this strict order? (27th)

Severe Frost and Hail Disaster in Shaanxi Province

No Harvest Expected in Guanzhong and Yulin

The Livelihood of the Surviving Victims Is Completely Cut Off

A dispatch from Xi'an states that Shaanxi Province has suffered from continuous drought for years, and the rural areas are bankrupt. Since the sowing of wheat seedlings last autumn, there has been a great lack of rain and snow, and most of the crops have withered. Fortunately, at the end of March, abundant rain fell, and the non-withered crops were able to be saved. It was expected that there would still be a harvest of 20% to 30% this summer, and the surviving people could recover slightly. Unexpectedly, at the beginning of May, they suffered from black frost, strong winds, and hail. Flying sand and stones caused houses to collapse, and wheat, beans, melons, and cotton were all destroyed. People were very panicked, and their livelihoods were completely cut off. Guanzhong and Yulin were completely affected by the disaster. The Provincial Relief Association has printed concise disaster information sheets for the affected counties to appeal to all parties. The disaster situation in each county is briefly recorded as follows: Sanyuan: Suffered from strong winds and black frost, and the wheat seedlings have withered. There is no hope for the summer harvest. Lintong: Suffered from strong winds, hail, snow, and frost, and the wheat and beans have withered. There is no hope for the summer harvest. Fengxiang: Suffered from strong winds and black frost, and the wheat seedlings are withered, causing panic among the people. Fufeng: Suffered from strong winds and severe frost, and the wheat and beans are withered and black. There is no hope for a harvest. Xingquan: Suffered from hurricanes and black frost, and the wheat seedlings are destroyed, causing panic among the people. Baishui: Suffered from strong winds and heavy snow, and the weather is cold, and most of the wheat and beans have withered. The people's livelihood has been cut off. Pucheng: Suffered from repeated wind disasters, and the wheat and beans have been blown off, causing the people to cry. Dali: Suffered from repeated storms, and houses have collapsed, and the seedlings of wheat, beans, melons, and cotton have withered, causing grain prices to skyrocket. Qishan: Suffered from storms and severe frost, and the wheat and beans have withered, causing grain prices to rise sharply. Gaoling: Suffered from black frost and wind disasters, and the crops have become dry. There is disappointment for the summer harvest. Chaoyi: Suffered from rain, hail, and black frost, and the wheat and beans have withered. There is no hope for a harvest. Huxian: Suffered from continuous ice, frost, and storms, and the crops are dry, causing disappointment for the summer harvest. Chengcheng: Suffered from strong winds, frost, and snow, and the weather is severely cold, and the crops are withered, and the houses have collapsed, making the disaster extremely severe. Weinan: Suffered from strong winds and black frost, and the wheat seedlings have completely withered, causing constant cries in the countryside. Huayin: Suffered from strong winds and severe frost, and the crops have withered. There is no hope for the summer harvest. Huaxian: The disaster situation is the same as Huayin. Pingmin: Suffered from black frost and strong winds, and the crops have been destroyed. There is no hope for the summer harvest. (The above counties belong to the Guanzhong Circuit.) Yijun: Suffered from storms and heavy snow, and the crops have been killed, causing disappointment for the harvest. (The above belongs to the Lin Yushou Circuit.) The surviving victims have suffered this strange disaster, and their livelihoods have been almost hopeless. (Shenshe News Agency)

Current Status of Inland Water Transportation in Sichuan

Chongqing Correspondence: River transportation in Sichuan relies solely on steamships and motorboats. Except for commercial steamers operating on the upper and lower reaches of the Yangtze River and motorboats on the Jialing River, the narrow and shallow waters of inland ports such as the Tuo River, Min River, and Jinsha River have prevented steamer traffic. Local Chinese merchants are currently making efforts to organize small steamers or motorboats to navigate these inland ports, aiming to facilitate inland transportation. The following is a compilation of information gathered regarding commercial steamers currently operating on Sichuan's inland waterways, for the reference of those interested in navigation:

(1) Emei: Shipowner: China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. Built in 1920. Displacement: 576 tons. Speed: 14 nautical miles per hour. Iron steam engine. Operates on the Chongqing-Yichang and Chongqing-Shanghai lines. Docked at the south bank of Chongqing.

(2) Fuyang: (Sanbei Company). Built in 1922. 475 tons. Speed: 14 nautical miles per hour. Iron construction. Steam engine. Operates on the Chongqing-Yichang and Chongqing-Shanghai lines. Docked at Huichuan Gate, Jiangbei.

(3) Wuxing: (Sanbei Company). Built in 1926. 371 tons. Speed: 14 nautical miles per hour. Construction, equipment, operating area, and docking location are the same as Fuyang.

(4) Wan'an: (Central Company). Built in 1925. 358 tons. Speed: 13.5 nautical miles per hour. Construction, equipment, and operating location are the same as above. Docked at Jialing Wharf, Chongqing.

(5) Yujiang: (Xiajiang Company). Built in 1925. 327 tons. Speed: 14.5 nautical miles per hour. Manufacturing equipment and docking location are the same as Wan'an.

(6) Yongnian: (Yongqing Company). Built in 1925. 534 tons. Speed: 15 nautical miles per hour. Construction, operating section, and docking location are the same as above.

(7) Shuan: (Chengdu Minsheng Transportation Company). Built in 1924. 180 tons. Speed: 14 nautical miles per hour. Construction and equipment are the same as above. Docked at Renhe Wharf, Chongqing.

(8) Yuantong: (Xinhua Company). Built in 1929. 166 tons. Speed: 10 nautical miles per hour. The rest is the same as above.

(9) Shutong: (Xinhua Company). Built in 1909 (Xuantong era). 37 tons. Speed: 12.5 nautical miles per hour. The rest is the same as above.

(10) Zhaotong: Shipowner: Xinhua Company. Built in 1921. 31 tons. Speed: 20 nautical miles per hour. Operates between Chongqing and Jiading.

(11) Nantong: (Xinhua Company). Built in 1925. 106 tons. Speed: 10.8 nautical miles per hour. Iron construction. Diesel engine. Operates on the Chongqing-Jialing line. Docking location is the same as above.

(12) Changan: (Changan Company). Built in 1925. 188 tons. Speed: 12.8 nautical miles per hour. Iron construction. Diesel engine. Operating area undefined.

(14) Hengda: (Hengda Company). Built in 1922. 71 tons. The rest is the same as Changan.

(15) Shudu: (Jiuyuan Company). Built in 1925. 125 tons. Speed: 12 nautical miles. The rest is the same as above.

(16) Yuchuan: (Longmen Company). Built in 1924. 125 tons. Docking location: Dongshuimen, Chongqing. The rest is the same as above.

(17) Tianfu: (Longmen Company). Year of manufacture unknown. 40 tons. Speed: 9.6 miles. Iron steam engine. The rest is the same as above.

(18) Yizhou: (Sanyi Company). Built in 1930. 018 tons. Speed: 9.8 miles. The rest is the same as before.

(19) Minsheng Company ships include Minsheng, Minyong, Minwang, Minfu, Minzhi, Minan, Minyou, Minheng, Minjiang, Minxuan, Minjue, Minyin, Minqiang, Minzhu, Minkang, Mingui, Minyue, Minning, Yongnian, etc., totaling 19 vessels. Most were built between 1921 and 1931. Except for Mingui, Yongnian, Minzhu, and Minkang, which are larger, most range from 188 tons to 7 tons. They operate on the Chongqing-Jialing, Chongqing-Hechuan, Chongqing-Wanxian, Chongqing-Yichang, Chongqing-Shanghai, and Chongqing-Hankou lines. In recent years, the company's business has been quite prosperous. In addition, on the Chongqing-Wanxian and Chongqing-Jialing lines, there are the Jiangjin Company's Jiangjin and Jiangyu ships, the Jiangyi Company's Jiangyi and Jiangtai, the Fujiang Company's Fujiang, the Qingci Company's Qingci and Qinghe, the Suining Company's Suining, the Yuqing Company's Yuqing, Xinyi, Yuanyuan, and Xujia, the Hengshan Company's Hengshan, etc., totaling 11 vessels. Except for Suining, most were built in recent years. Among them, in addition to operating on the Chongqing-Wanxian and Chongqing-Jialing lines, they also navigate the Chongqing-Hechuan area. The tonnage is mostly between 50 tons and 3 tons. In total, the number of commercial steamers on Sichuan's inland rivers is approximately 47. All of them are solely funded by Chinese merchants, with no foreign capital. As for foreign commercial steamers operating on Sichuan's inland rivers, there are the British Swire Company's Wanliu, Wanxian, Wantong, Youyang, Xiushan, and Tuoqian, the American Yangtze River Steamship Company's Qichun, Qiping, and Qianan, Jardine Matheson's Chuandong, Chuannan, and Chuanbei, the Japanese Nisshin Kisen's Yunyang Maru, Yiyang Maru, and Deyang Maru, as well as ships from Italy, France, Germany, Belgium, Denmark, and the Netherlands, all operating in various parts of Sichuan's inland rivers.

Hopeful Resolution for Waterway Disputes in Northern Shandong

Construction Department Plans to Renovate Canal Dikes

Jinan Correspondence: Zhang Honglie, Director of the Construction Department, previously went to Enxian and Wucheng counties to investigate disputes arising from the construction of river dikes. He also studied solutions with local officials and residents from both counties. He returned to Jinan last night. Today, Mr. Zhang went to the Provincial Government to meet Chairman Han Fuqu, reporting on the investigation of the canal and the process of consulting local opinions for solutions. It was generally agreed that renovating the canal dikes was necessary to resolve the disputes. Mr. Han agreed and decided that the Provincial Government would subsidize 10,000 yuan, while Enxian and Wucheng counties would each raise 5,000 yuan to complete the project. After returning to the department, Zhang Honglie instructed his staff to draft detailed plans overnight, aiming to submit them to the Provincial Government tomorrow. This afternoon, the reporter visited Zhang at the Construction Department, inquiring about the meeting with Han and the content of the solutions. According to Mr. Zhang, "The dispute between Enxian and Wucheng counties stems from flooding. If we renovate the canal dikes once and for all, we can avoid flooding and naturally resolve the disputes. Because the dikes of the Northern Canal have too many bends, the water flow is not smooth. There are more than a dozen dangerous sections on the eastern bank of the canal near the junction of Enxian and Wucheng counties. During the continuous rains of summer, the river dikes collapse, flooding Enxian from the Sha River. Enxian then builds dikes to block the Sha River water, harming Wucheng, hence the disputes. Previously, Wucheng allowed Enxian to build dikes, stipulating that the height should not exceed six feet, but during heavy rains, the highest water level of the canal reaches two and a half meters. A six-foot dike, of course, cannot stop the water, and the disputes cannot be resolved, and have recently escalated, leading to armed clashes and tragic loss of life. This time, I personally went to Enxian and Wucheng counties, convened meetings with the people, explained the importance of righteousness, and studied solutions with the two county magistrates. Fortunately, everyone was able to set aside their biases and was willing to work together to renovate the canal dikes and permanently eliminate flooding. Enxian must help Wucheng, and Wucheng must also help Enxian. However, both counties are inherently poor. Enxian has already levied 15 or 16 yuan per mu, which is already unsustainable. If we want to complete this project, we must rely on the Provincial Government for assistance. I have just met with Chairman Han, who has decided to order Enxian and Wucheng counties to each contribute 5,000 yuan, and the province will subsidize 10,000 yuan, making 20,000 yuan as construction costs, with the two counties providing labor to complete the work. As for the detailed plans, the department is currently drafting them and will be completed tomorrow. If we can start construction soon, Enxian and Wucheng counties can be free from flooding this year, and there will be no more disputes," and so on. (27th)

Anhui Provincial Government Investigates Wuhu

Case of Illegal Sale of National Territory

Wuhu Correspondence: Although Wuhu is one of the trading ports in the Yangtze River basin, it still lacks a concession in the treaty system. However, in recent years, excellent areas near the wharves along the river, such as Shishan Mountain, Shizi Mountain, Fenghuang Mountain, Qingshan Mountain, Tieshan Mountain, and along the Xijiang River, have been occupied by foreigners under the guise of foreign firms, companies, schools, hospitals, residential villas, and so on. Through gradual encroachment and annexation, these areas have long become special regions, significantly affecting Wuhu's commerce and culture. In June of last year, the Wuhu Orphanage, citing financial difficulties, attempted to privately sell 40 mu of land located along the Xijiang River to the Texaco Oil Company to build oil storage tanks. After learning of this, various sectors believed that it would not only harm territorial sovereignty but also that the oil storage tanks would affect local public safety, and filed petitions with the provincial government, as well as the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Industry, requesting strict prohibition. Only then was the matter averted. Recently, a Hong, in collusion with Tang Jinzhou and others, fabricated the names of three households, Tang Jingji, Tang Jingshentang, and Xue Yuji, to purchase dozens of mu of land along the Xijiang River and then illegally sell it to a merchant from a certain country. They also obtained a certificate from Zhou Mengwen, the manager of Li Bohang, a major landlord in Wuhu, to vouch for them at the county government, and paid the tax on the land deed. The county government initially believed that it was a transfer of property rights between people of the same country and collected the tax according to regulations, without refusing. Soon after, the county party headquarters and various sectors discovered that these individuals were actively proceeding with the resale to a certain foreign national after obtaining the tax deed, which caused great astonishment. They immediately submitted petitions to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of Industry, the Anhui Provincial Government, and the Provincial Party Headquarters, requesting prompt investigation and prohibition to protect sovereignty. After receiving the petitions, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Industry telegraphed the Anhui Provincial Government to quickly investigate the truth. The provincial government and the provincial party headquarters dispatched Ye Renshan, director of the fourth section of the construction department, to Wuhu to investigate the matter. He is currently reviewing the case files and conducting on-site inspections in order to report back. (24th)

Nanhui

Three Robbers Executed by Firing Squad

On the night of January 20th of this year, Li Lianhai's home in the northwest of Xinchang was suddenly attacked by robbers Zhou Rongsheng, Zhang Gengsheng, Wang Quansheng, Huang Ayin, Hu Gengquan, and others, who banded together, armed with weapons, stealing silver coins, jewelry, and other valuables worth over 600 yuan, and fled after dividing the loot. After interrogation, they confessed to conspiring with Huang Ayin and Hu Gengquan, who were still at large, to commit the robbery. They were sentenced to death and the sentence was submitted to the provincial government for approval. Yesterday morning, the three criminals were brought from the county prison, their identities were verified, and they were tied up and taken to the execution ground outside the south gate to be executed by firing squad.

Provincial Order Strictly Pursues Old Taxes, Urging Payment of Grain Tribute

Since taking office, the newly appointed County Magistrate of this county, Yan Shenyu, has repeatedly received provincial orders to strictly pursue old tax arrears and urgently remit them to the province within a specified period. After receiving the order, Magistrate Yan summoned all the heads of the districts in the county to the county government for a lecture, strictly pursuing old arrears and detaining four district chiefs, including Sun Tingzhen, who had accumulated large arrears, and recovering the payments. Yesterday, Magistrate Yan ordered Zhu Kaiguan, Director of Land Tax, to strictly pursue payments within a limited time. Director Zhu, upon receiving the order, has already instructed the various tax collectors to strictly pursue them.

Supervisory Institute Secretly Investigates Riot by Refugees

In February of this year, more than 160 refugees from Shouzhou, northern Anhui, arrived at Yanjiaqiao, Tangxiangbian, District 8 of this county and wantonly caused disturbances. The town's chamber of commerce came forward to dissuade them, but the refugees refused to comply. The chamber of commerce fired warning shots into the sky, and stray bullets injured the refugees Zhang Yude and others. Zhang and others reported the injuries to the county court prosecutor's office for examination and accused the chamber of commerce members of attempted murder. After investigation, the prosecutor's office concluded that the chamber of commerce members did not use excessive force for self-defense and decided not to prosecute. However, at the time of the incident, the Anhui Fellow-Provincials Association repeatedly submitted appeals to various departments and commissions of the Central National Government and various agencies of the provincial government. After receiving the report, Yu Youren, the President of the Supervisory Yuan, specially sent his secretary, Mr. Wang Jingqing, to Wuxi to secretly investigate. He went to the county court to review the submissions from both sides and the testimonies of various people, and visited Tangxiangbian, the site of the incident, the ancient temple that housed the refugees, Dr. Chen Shuliang, who treated the refugees, and the 16th branch of the Public Security Bureau in charge of the area, to investigate the circumstances of the disturbance at the time and the police's suppression efforts. He conducted a thorough investigation, stayed in Wuxi for three days, and returned to Nanjing yesterday to report back.

Changzhou

Approval Granted to Add Rickshaws

The case of adding rickshaws in Wu County has been brewing for a long time. Recently, the provincial government finally approved the opening, ordering the county to properly prepare a plan for implementation. It is now known that the county government yesterday announced the method of adding rickshaws, opening up 100 in the urban area and 200 on various roads. All those who have previously applied for registration should go to the county from June 1st to the 15th of this year to register and claim the number of vehicles, prepare cash according to the price of 60 yuan per vehicle and a public welfare donation of 120 yuan, and submit it to the designated local five banks, China Communications, Farmers, Jiangsu, and Shanghai, for storage. The county will send personnel to check that it matches, approve the registration, and issue a certificate. Then, according to the registered number, the vehicles will be distributed proportionally, and a lottery will be held publicly on a separate date.

Zhenjiang

Construction Department Actively Prevents Rice Borers and Locusts

The Jiangsu Construction Department recently noted that many locust nymphs had occurred in Lishui, Jiangpu, Gaoyou, Guanyun, Dongtai, Funing and other counties, causing extreme harm. It has drafted an outline for the implementation of pest control work in the whole province this year, and plans to set up 14 pest control instructors and assistants to be sent to various counties to guide farmers in locust control and rice borer control work together with the county governments. It also plans to set up a test area each in Jiangnan and Jiangbei, with two technicians and two assistants each, to test the methods of locust control and rice borer control. All the work is scheduled for six months, with a budget of 23,000 yuan, which is proposed to be submitted to the Provincial Government for discussion. Once approved, it will be implemented immediately.

Rugao

Farmer Commits Suicide Due to Poverty

A farmer named Pan Man in Huajiazhuang, Chemahu District, was impoverished. He had a wife and two children, and they struggled to make a living. At this time of year, when the new and old harvests were not yet joined, the family had run out of food and grass. The family of four had been without food for three days. The wife cried and the children wailed, which was unbearable to hear. Pan, in a moment of despair, conceived a thought of world-weariness, so on the previous (23rd) day, he took advantage of his wife's absence and hanged himself with a hemp rope. Although both children were by his side, they were young and did not know how to call for help. By the time his wife returned home, he had already breathed his last. It was truly tragic.

Yangmu Township Robbery of Egg Shop

At 3 am on the 23rd, six or seven bandits suddenly came to Wu Taihe's egg shop in Yangmu Township, Shuangdian District, broke in and entered, holding weapons such as box guns, flashlights, and short knives. There were only a 16-year-old child and his partner Xu in the shop. The bandits pointed the box guns at them and forced them to hand over silver coins. They were robbed of 96 yuan in silver coins and 230,000 copper coins, and left after firing shots and shouting.

Pinghu

Citizens Indict Former County Magistrate Wu

Zheng Zhong, the head of the dispatch department of this county, committed suicide by smoking opium after being slapped and intimidated by County Magistrate Wu Wentai. This has already been reported in this newspaper. Wu has now been transferred to Shanghai. The family of the deceased, through mediation by others, withdrew the charges. Citizens such as Lin Dalun were greatly dissatisfied upon hearing this and immediately telegraphed the High Court, requesting a fair trial in accordance with the law. A full transcript of the original telegram is provided below. "To the esteemed High Court: The case of Wu Wentai, the former magistrate of Pinghu County, forcing dispatch clerk Zheng Zhong to commit suicide upon his departure, has caused a public outcry in the local and Shanghai-Hangzhou newspapers. The family of the deceased, Zheng Hu, has already filed a complaint with Examiner Chen, who confirmed the facts, and sent a telegram to your court requesting a thorough investigation. It has now come to our attention that Wu Wentai, knowing that he cannot escape the law, has instigated local bullies such as Xu Meixuan to coerce and lure the family of the deceased to withdraw the charges, which is clearly a private settlement of a murder case and a great violation of the law. As this case falls purely within the scope of criminal law, it cannot be freely started or stopped. Fearing that officials will protect each other and the spirit of the law will be lost, we, the citizens, dare not remain silent. We hereby telegraph you to reject the request to withdraw the charges and to promptly designate jurisdiction to conduct a fair trial to comfort the wronged soul and rectify official corruption."

More Than Twenty Japanese Warships Move to Longshan

The five Japanese warships previously docked in Zhapu have now sailed south. According to reports from travelers returning from Dinghai, they witnessed the warships docking near Sijiao Mountain and Huanglong Mountain, with a total of more than twenty ships.

Large Gangs of Robbers Rampage in Maokou

Wang Yanming, a resident of Maokou in the northern border of this county, whose home had self-defense guns, was coveted by robbers. The night before, more than 30 bandits with white cloths wrapped around their heads, each armed with guns, crowded into his home and robbed him of four long and short guns, as well as gold rings, gold rings, silver coins, and other items. Wang's brother sneaked out and fired a shot, and the robbers fled.

Xiaoshan

Robbery and Assault Case at Xiajiaqiao

On the evening of the 25th, several robbers suddenly came to the Tian family near Xiajiaqiao in Xiaoshan, first imprisoning seven members of the Tian family, including women and children, in a room, then going upstairs to search and loot. They stole five silk garments, four gold rings, one pearl hat, and more than 50 yuan in cash. They also burned a 70-year-old mother with fire.

Ningbo

Major Fire in Shiqiu Street, Zhenhai

Zhang Xiaosheng's cake shop in Shiqiu Street, Jianyan District, Zhenhai, had a 60-year-old mother who, on the previous (23rd) day at 11:00 am, accidentally started a fire while cooking soybeans, causing the roof to burn through. By the time the fire engines from various villages rushed to the rescue, five single-story houses and thirteen rooms, seven two-story houses and ten rooms, and a water pavilion had been burned down. In addition, two beams of the stone bridge were broken. It is estimated that the losses amounted to approximately 70,000 yuan, with Li Changxing's grocery store suffering the most significant losses, estimated at around 30,000 yuan.

Chinese Nationals Trafficking Military Weapons

Three Arrested on French Mail Ship

Marseille: Three Chinese nationals were arrested on the French Mail Ship Company's "Athos" en route to Saigon for trafficking military weapons. All the weapons were stored in full packages, with each package containing ten pistols and one thousand rounds of ammunition. The hiding place was behind the iron plates near the engine room. After being arrested, the traffickers confessed that part of the weapons would be delivered in Saigon and part in Shanghai. Their method was to hide each package of weapons inside a car tire, tie it with a long rope and cork, so that it would not sink when thrown into the sea, and the receiver could come and collect it. However, the traffickers refused to confess who was instructing them. (27th Havas dispatch)

After Takahashi Decides to Stay On

Japanese Political Situation Remains Unstable

Seiyukai Tries Hard to Make Things Difficult for Saitō

Tokyo Dispatch from the Japan United News Agency, 28th – Although the political world temporarily stabilized after Finance Minister Takahashi decided to stay on, the Seiyukai Party is extremely indignant towards the government, and as a result, the political situation has once again fallen into an unstable state. The Seiyukai Party is now divided into two factions internally. One faction advocates for an immediate break with the current cabinet, while the other believes that the time is not yet ripe and prefers to adopt a self-restrained attitude and observe the situation quietly. However, the influence of the pro-break faction is gradually increasing, so President Suzuki has not dared to make a definitive decision lightly. Those who want to maintain the current cabinet, those who want to take advantage of the Seiyukai Party's tough attitude, and those who are trying to realize the Suzuki cabinet, the Hiranuma cabinet, and the Ugaki cabinet are all conducting separate activities. However, the government side, because of Takahashi's determination to fulfill his mission, believes that even if the Seiyukai Party breaks away, it will not be difficult to reorganize the cabinet, and they remain optimistic. Therefore, the political situation can be maintained for the time being. However, when it comes to compiling the budget, there will inevitably be a considerable amount of tension between the government and the Seiyukai Party.

Tokyo Dispatch from the Japan United News Agency, 28th – Although the Japanese political world is currently stable, its future is clouded by dark clouds and does not allow for optimism. According to observations from various factions, the future trend of the political situation is as follows: (1) The House of Peers, President Suzuki, and the government are at odds, and Finance Minister Takahashi's feelings have worsened since Takahashi stayed on as finance minister. However, the Seiyukai Party is divided internally, so the issue of a break cannot be easily implemented. Prime Minister Saitō and President Suzuki should decide on their attitudes early and strive to dispel the dark clouds. (2) The Minseitō Party believes that the Seiyukai Party currently lacks a great politician who can see through the political situation, so they cannot decide on a definite attitude until the time comes to compile the budget. If the Seiyukai Party implements a break at that time, the Minseitō Party will uphold the current cabinet according to its established policy, exclude the Seiyukai Party's conspiracy, and do its best to make it easier for Saitō to reorganize the cabinet. Therefore, no matter what attitude the Seiyukai Party takes, the political situation will not undergo major changes. (3) The Kokumin Domei Party believes that the party is the only opposition party and has always firmly believed that a political upheaval will occur during the budget compilation period. Therefore, the party is united as one to prepare to take over the cabinet.

Tokyo Dispatch from the Dentsu News Agency, 28th – The young and radical members of the Seiyukai Party will hold a meeting of members tomorrow at 1:00 p.m. to express their tough stance of immediately breaking away from the current cabinet and urge President Suzuki to make a decision.

Tokyo Dispatch from the Dentsu News Agency, 28th – Seiyukai President Suzuki is paying close attention to the trends of the radical and self-restrained factions within the party, and has ordered the leaders of Shimada, Matsuno, Yamazaki, and others to visit the party elders to gather information. However, the general trend of the party is that the argument for immediate disaffiliation is gradually gaining strength. If there is a major cause, even those who advocate self-restraint will not strongly oppose immediate disaffiliation. President Suzuki seems to have realized this and made a decision internally, so the period for the Seiyuukai to sever ties with the government may be brought forward, and it may be carried out before the budget is compiled, as early as late June.

Tokyo Dispatch from the Dentsu News Agency, 28th – The Kokumin Domei Party held a general assembly today at 3:00 p.m. President Adachi and Secretary-General Yamamichi, Nakano, Kiyose, Furuya, and others discussed countermeasures to the current situation. At that time, President Adachi's speech was as follows: The speculation that Finance Minister Takahashi's agreement to stay on has allowed the Saitō cabinet to be maintained and the political situation to stabilize belongs to the legal community. The political situation is of course even more unstable, and the existing political parties will tend to collapse. It is a mistake to say that the extraordinary situation has now been resolved and we have returned to the normal path of constitutionalism, or to say that the extraordinary situation has not yet been resolved, so the current cabinet should be maintained. The credibility of political parties has not yet been restored in any way. At the same time, there are those who advocate that the current situation is extraordinary and the cabinet should be changed. However, if the situation is extraordinary, the incompetent and inactive cabinet should be overthrown, the political parties should be reformed, and we should move forward to establish countermeasures for an extraordinary situation.

Mastermind of Assassination Plot Against Saitō

Sentenced to One and a Half Years in Prison, Suspended for Two Years

Tokyo Dispatch from the Japan United News Agency, 28th – Imamaki Yoshio, a medical doctor and member of the Shinbu Society who masterminded the plot to assassinate Prime Minister Saitō, was sentenced by the presiding judge at the Tokyo District Court on the 27th to one year and six months in prison, suspended for two years.

Austria-Germany Discord Intensifies

Hitler's Party Members Demand Austrian Chancellor's Resignation

Berlin Dispatch from Reuters, 27th – The Austrian government's plan to suppress the National Socialist Party has aroused the anger of the German National Socialist Party. As a retaliatory measure, the German government is charging German citizens traveling to Austria a passport fee of 1,000 marks. At the same time, the headquarters of the National Socialist Party issued a declaration demanding the resignation of Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss and the formation of a government of national concentration, saying that without this, there would be no way to maintain Austria's economic, political, and cultural security. Dr. Goebbels originally intended to travel to Rome via Austria, but has now decided not to pass through Vienna and will fly directly to Rome tonight.

Vienna Dispatch from the National News Agency, 27th – When Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss went to the university today to participate in a memorial service held by the Catholic Student Association for soldiers who died in the European War, several disputes arose among the students, and they even fought in front of the Chancellor. The Chancellor then left the venue immediately and refused to attend. The university has been temporarily closed.

Berlin Dispatch from the National News Agency, 27th – The German government has newly ordered that all German people who wish to transit to Guangdong must pay an exit passport fee of 1,000 marks, which, at the current exchange rate, is approximately 70 gold pounds. This harsh order is tantamount to severing traffic between Germany and Austria, so that, apart from border merchants who can continue to travel between the two countries, all other travelers are completely banned. The biggest reason for this move is that the animosity between the German and Austrian governments is deepening day by day, and the authorities are particularly hostile to figures of the National Socialist Party, resulting in the promulgation of a law prohibiting them from wearing National Socialist Party uniforms and badges. The German authorities, in view of this, and because it is difficult to distinguish whether Germans passing through Austria are members of the National Socialist Party, have decided to adopt a heavy tax system for the convenience of management and to avoid unfortunate incidents between Germans and the Austrian government, in order to show that the prohibition is implicit in the tax.

Vienna Dispatch from the National News Agency, 27th – The German government's new order requiring those leaving the country to Austria to pay an exit passport fee of 1,000 marks has greatly surprised the Austrian government. It is said that a countermeasure plan will be taken to prohibit the transfer of mark accounts. This move will greatly hinder commercial relations between the two countries.

The German Crisis Is Still Deeply Hidden (Berlin Correspondence)

Unemployment Has Not Decreased, Entrepreneurs' Debts Have Increased

The Government Is Heavily Indebted, and the Disarmament Problem Is the Most Difficult to Solve

It has been almost four months since Hitler came to power. How are his political achievements? It will not be seen until after his four-year term. We cannot see it now. However, when he came to power, he promoted three major agendas. The first was to reform the chaotic labor organization, especially to suppress the Communist Party. The second was to restore the harmonious movement between labor and capital. The third was to increase the internal strength of all industrial sectors. These are the economic policies that the German Federal Economic Conference has passed to be thoroughly implemented.

Now the activities of the Communist Party have stopped on the surface, and the books of Marx, Lenin, and even Kautsky cannot be sold publicly. The labor organization has almost become an underground movement, and even the trade unions led by the Social Democratic Party have been greatly destroyed, and they are also considered to be contrary to the German "national spirit." However, the poverty situation in the rural areas may actually be better than that of our motherland, the Republic of China, but we have never seen or heard of any emergency relief measures. Therefore, the prices of agricultural products are very different from the prices of industrial products. For example, in the price index in March of this year, the wholesale price of agricultural products (assuming 1913 is 100) was 81.6 in March of this year, while the price of refined industrial products maintained a high level of 111.5. The decline of animal husbandry is even more serious than that of agriculture. Therefore, the Hitler government is studying how to raise the prices of butter and milk. The reason is that relieving the rural areas and revitalizing the rural areas means directly finding outlets for industrial products and opening up the domestic market. Only one-fifth of German industrial products are sold to farmers, so the recovery of rural areas has a great impact on industry. However, the German government's ability to implement this is still a question. Moreover, the unemployed masses are in the same position as the farmers and are suffering a tragic fate. If we want to talk about restoring market prosperity, we must not let the more than six million unemployed masses take their own course and stand idly by. Therefore, successive German governments have paid great attention to this and have done their best to invest huge amounts of money to relieve the unemployed. Recently, Hitler has proposed 125 million marks from the national treasury to help the unemployed find work in public works projects. Its effectiveness is almost the same as the American "Civilian Conservation Corps" organization for 250,000 unemployed workers. The scope is narrow, and the number of people who are relieved is limited compared to the total number of unemployed. He wants to recruit the unemployed masses from all over the streets and lanes, and at the same time use public welfare to encourage the masses to improve the government's ability to implement economic policies and its credibility, and to harvest the greatest effect with the least amount of labor in economic theory.

Hitler's real power is much greater than the dictatorial power given to the US President by the US Congress. All the national institutions within the German Federation are at Hitler's disposal, and he also has a Minister of Propaganda who often orders the government and its policies to be promoted, awakening public opinion, and focusing on the tasks designated by the government.

However, the German economy has shown signs of rising since February of this year, and the market has gradually turned around. However, to what extent the new forces can reach is still unpredictable. Therefore, what will the first stage of economic recovery look like? How much automatic recovery and adjustment capacity does the economy have? No one dares to make a rash judgment. Moreover, there are still many hidden dangers in front of us.

First, the purchasing power of the general public is still very low and is not easy to recover for a while, let alone exceed the previous level.

Second, the reduction of the unemployed masses is only due to seasonal factors, and it is not necessarily better than the same period last year, so it will inevitably be worse after this summer than last year.

Third, the burden of debt on entrepreneurs is increasing day by day. Borrowing new debts to repay old debts is definitely not a way out, and foreign trade has not improved. Germany is also a country that exports more than it imports. Even if the World Economic Conference discusses a fairly appropriate method, it may not be exactly what Germany needs. Then the German business community may not have hope of revival. Fourth, although reparations have been suspended, they can be said to be virtually suspended. However, Germany's total foreign debt is 22.8 billion marks. Even if political debt is excluded, it is still 21.3 billion marks. Taking its opponent as an example, the United Kingdom's foreign debt is only 10 billion marks, and France's is only 12 billion marks. How can such a huge debt be repaid?

The last one is a world problem, and it is also the most difficult, most difficult, and most dangerous disarmament problem between Germany and France. German citizens, especially members of the National Socialist Party and quasi-National Socialist Party members, believe that highly armed countries (such as France) are unwilling to reduce their armaments, so they ignore Germany's demand for equality in armaments. Germany insists on "equality in armaments," otherwise it will automatically deny the Treaty of Versailles and increase its armaments according to its capacity. However, from the perspective of France or the United Kingdom, Germany's 100,000 national defense forces have a service period of up to seven years, and their training subjects are all subjects of the school. The materials for German military weapons are also very good. At the same time, the National Socialist Party has assault teams, and the National People's Party has iron helmet regiments. They have all fully implemented military training. Even if they cannot be considered a formal combat army, they can awaken the narrow patriotic spirit of their general public, thereby causing a political crisis in Europe. In fact, even if Germany itself realizes "equality in armaments," it will only increase the burden on the people. Everyone knows that real welfare is very unreliable and there is a risk of causing great disaster. However, there is absolutely no freedom of speech in Germany today, so no one dares to mention it, let alone oppose equality in armaments. We can only let the crisis increase. (April 30, 1933, in Berlin)

Mr. Wang Shuhan arrived in Ping from Tianjin this morning. Wang Kemin stumbled at Fengzeyuan before, broke his glasses, and one eye was injured by the glass. He was admitted to Peking Union Medical College Hospital for treatment. He had surgery once, and the glass is still in his eye. After doctors and Wang's family members discussed the results, he will have another surgery within this week and will be difficult to be discharged from the hospital for a while. Therefore, the organization of the political and financial groups must be agreed upon with Mr. Wang Shuhan and Mr. Wang Kemin before a decision can be made. As for the monthly expenses of the Pingzheng Council, the central government will allocate 40,000 yuan per month. It is reported that the chairmen of the provinces in North China have decided to rush to arrive on June 1 to participate in the opening ceremony. The members in Tianjin and Shanghai have been invited by the Pingzheng Council and can arrive in Ping within the next few days. (May 26th)

Actions of Japanese Warships in Hankou

Hankou Dispatch: The commander of the Japanese First Overseas Dispatch Fleet, Sakano Tsunezen, previously went from Hankou to Yichang and Chongqing for inspection, surveying the situation along the Yangtze River and spying on our movements. After returning to Hankou, he immediately convened a secret meeting and decided to redeploy defenses along the upper reaches of the Yangtze River. The warships Ataka, Uji, Futami, Tsushima, Sumida, Atami, and Kotaka were stationed, and the 24th Destroyer Squadron's Momo, Yanagi, Kashi, and Yari were sent to Yichang. The Fushimi warship was sent to Changsha, and the Katada warship was sent to Huangshi Port. They are paying particular attention to all our military intelligence and are sparing no effort in attempting to gather it. At a time when there are widespread rumors of ceasefire negotiations in North China, the Japanese still have such actions in the heart of the Yangtze River, which is enough to show that their schemes against us are truly all-encompassing. Today is Japanese Navy Day. All officers and soldiers of the Japanese warships docked in Hankou, as well as Japanese residents in Hankou, held a celebration at the Naval Assembly Hall in the Japanese Concession at 1:00 PM. Commander Sakano, Army Attaché Muto, Consul General Shimizu, Vice-Consul Tanaka, and others all gave speeches. At the same time, the warships fired celebratory salutes to mark the occasion. (27th)

Local News

### May Thirtieth Memorial

Memorial Meeting Convened by All Sectors

Half-Mast Throughout the City, Entertainment Suspended

Tomorrow is the eighth anniversary of the May Thirtieth Massacre. The City Party Headquarters has decided to convene a memorial meeting of all sectors at 9:00 AM. All government agencies will still operate as usual. Details are as follows:

Memorial Meeting Held by All Sectors

The City Party Headquarters considers the May Thirtieth Massacre to be a significant memorial day for the revolutionary movement.

It has decided to convene a memorial meeting of all sectors at 10:00 AM tomorrow morning on the third floor of the Party Headquarters to commemorate the eighth anniversary of the May Thirtieth Massacre. All agencies, organizations, schools, and party headquarters at all levels have been notified to send two representatives with letters of credentials to participate in the commemoration.

Half-Mast Throughout the City to Express Grief

All sectors in the city, as the May Thirtieth Massacre occurred on Nanjing Road in this city, to commemorate the martyred heroes and express condolences, will fly flags at half-mast for one day. All amusement parks and cinemas are ordered to suspend performances and entertainment to show mourning.

Agencies Operate as Usual

All agencies under the jurisdiction of the Municipal Government, district party headquarters under the jurisdiction of the City Party Headquarters, the Garrison Headquarters, and the courts will operate as usual. All schools will also hold classes as usual and will not give holidays.

Public Cemetery Board Performs Public Memorial Ceremony

More than 20 students and citizens were unfortunately killed in the May Thirtieth Massacre. Afterwards, all sectors raised funds to build the May Thirtieth Martyrs' Cemetery in the Fangjia Wood Bridge area of Zhabei. Yu Qiaqing, Cheng Xieshun, and others were elected as directors to organize a board of directors to manage it. The board holds a public memorial ceremony every year on May 30th to remember the event. This year is another anniversary, and the board has specifically notified all directors to go to the cemetery at 9:00 AM tomorrow morning to perform the public memorial ceremony. A preparatory meeting has been held to determine the ceremony's format and prepare a memorial address, etc.

Temporary Martial Law in the Chinese Area

The Chinese Concession Police Authorities received a confidential report stating that reactionary elements will hold gatherings and parades tomorrow. Therefore, in accordance with the martial law measures for the May Revolution Memorial Day, temporary martial law will be implemented starting tonight. The Municipal Public Security Bureau, led by Director Wen, has instructed all police personnel under its jurisdiction to go on duty. Double posts have been added to all major roads, and police have been dispatched to protect the intersection of the Chinese Concession, the Public Sports Ground on Avenue Haig, Zhonghua Road, and all important public institutions. Inspectors, detectives, and female inspectors have been dispatched to inspect pedestrians on all roads. Police brigades and patrol car teams have been dispatched to patrol all roads. The Garrison Headquarters and patrol teams have also been dispatched to patrol the Nanshi area. The Municipal Government has also stationed a large security team. Soldiers from the Longhua Garrison Headquarters are also standing guard nearby. The High Chang Temple is under the strict protection of naval guards. Members of the Municipal Defense Corps will all go on duty to assist in defense.

Precautions in the Two Concessions

The authorities of the Public Concession, as the May Thirtieth Memorial is directly related to the Concession, are taking particularly strict precautions. All Chinese and foreign detectives in all police stations have been ordered to go on duty starting at 12:00 AM tonight. Red alert vehicles have been dispatched to patrol all important locations. Factories are densely located in eastern and western Shanghai, with a large number of workers, so vigilance is even tighter. All police stations in the French Concession have also been ordered to go on duty, and Vietnamese police have been added at the intersection of the Chinese Concession to inspect pedestrians. If necessary, the iron gates at the intersection will be closed.

Feng Yuxiang Issues a Circular Telegram Firmly Advocating Resistance Against Japan

General Feng Yuxiang assumed the position of Commander-in-Chief of the People's Anti-Japanese Allied Army in Zhangjiakou on the 26th of this month and issued a circular telegram to the whole country, stating in essence: Japanese imperialism's aggression against China is intensifying, with the ultimate goal of destroying our country and enslaving our nation, which will never change. Recently, the entire Great Wall line has been lost, and enemy forces are attacking Pingjin, publicly stating that they will take Zhangjiakou. Not only is Hebei and Chahar in danger, but everything north of the Yellow River will be lost. Yuxiang has been residing in Zhangjiakou for several months. Citizens and organizations from Pingjin, Shanghai, Guangdong, and other provinces have frequently sent messengers and telegrams, urging him to uphold righteousness and resist Japan. Yuxiang deeply believes that resisting foreign aggression and saving the country is the common responsibility and obligation of every citizen. Considering his own lack of talent and strength, he dares not avoid death and seek a life of ease. He respectfully obeys the expectations of the people in various regions and, on May 26, 1933, in the capacity of a citizen, assumed the position of Commander-in-Chief of the People's Anti-Japanese Allied Army on the front lines of Chahar Province, leading like-minded soldiers and civilians to form an anti-Japanese front, armed to defend Chahar Province, recover lost territory, and strive for China's independence and freedom. He will use every bit of strength he has, and he will give his all, even to death.

Su Zongjun and Others to Go to Hong Kong Tomorrow Morning to Welcome Him

According to the Riri News, Su Zongjun, the son of General Su Bingwen, Commander-in-Chief of the Northeast People's National Salvation Army, and representative Fan Ruizheng, etc., went south from Ping to Beijing to visit important figures in the central government and report. The brigade commander is Tang Zongxin, and the regimental commanders are Li Chunyan, Chang Baozhen, and Guan Yuxiang. The troops number 3,800 soldiers, and only 70-80% of them have guns. They are now under the control of Liu Yifei, Commander-in-Chief of the North China Advancement Army. All the troops have been fighting hard for many years, and they are experiencing difficulties with clothing and supplies. The soldiers are still wearing old fur coats and cannot replace them, which shows how difficult their situation is.

General Su, along with General Ma Zhanshan and others, will arrive in Hong Kong on the third of next month on the Conte Rosso of the Italian Mailboat Company. Da Nengxing Company Report

Hesun Steamer Robbed

More Than a Dozen Passengers Kidnapped, Huge Losses

Company Has Telegraphed Military and Police Authorities to Pursue Vigorously

The Hesun steamer of the Da Nengxing Steamboat Company on Tiantang Street in this port was robbed by pirates outside Dagukou on the 21st of this month while sailing from Tianjin to Yingkou. More than a dozen passengers were kidnapped. The steamer has safely arrived in Yingkou. Details are as follows:

Pirates Robbed

The Hesun steamer of the Da Nengxing Company in Yingkou, carrying 1,100 tons, sailed from Tianjin to Yingkou on the evening of the 21st. Pirates disguised as passengers mixed in. When the steamer sailed outside Dagukou, the pirates launched an attack, first forcing the captain to turn the steamer towards the Bohai Sea and began to rob at the same time. The steamer was full of passengers who were fleeing the serious situation in Tianjin. All their clothes and silver were robbed. On the morning of the 22nd, the pirates took the robbed property and boarded a prepared small steamer and left. The steamer then sailed to Yingkou. Before leaving, the pirates kidnapped more than a dozen passengers. The names and the exact number of passengers kidnapped are unknown, but it is known that the losses were huge.

Company Telegrams to Inquire

The Hesun steamer was originally scheduled to arrive in Yingkou on the 22nd. When the steamer did not arrive on time, the Yingkou head office was very worried and immediately telegraphed the Tianjin, Dalian, and Shanghai branch offices and various customs offices to inquire. It was not until the evening of the 24th that the Hesun steamer safely arrived in Yingkou. The head office, in addition to telegramming the military and police authorities in Tianjin and Dagukou to vigorously pursue the pirates and rescue the kidnapped passengers, also telegraphed Shanghai to report the details.

Levying Anti-Dumping Duties on Foreign Goods

Determined Types to Be Implemented

Detailed Rules for Collection Have Been Submitted to the Executive Yuan for Approval

After approval, collection may begin in the middle of next month. The Ministries of Industry and Finance, in order to restrict the dumping of foreign goods, have specially created anti-dumping duties on foreign goods. The two ministries have organized foreign goods dumping situation and have transferred it to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to order consuls stationed abroad to investigate the prices of goods nearby to determine whether they belong to dumping. It is now known that the investigation procedures have been completed, and the full text of the detailed rules for collection have also been drafted. The two ministries have submitted it to the Executive Yuan for review. Once passed, it will be announced by order of the Executive Yuan, and the customs offices throughout the country will begin collecting. However, it is heard that the collection standard for this anti-dumping duty is not universal for all goods, but only limited to foreign goods that conflict with our domestic products and hinder the sales of domestic goods. The ones that have been determined to be collected are cotton yarn, silk, tea, cloth, rice, wheat, timber, fish, light bulbs, matches, and other ten types. As for other necessary foreign goods, import duties will still be collected as usual, without collecting anti-dumping duties. As for the date of implementation, it is heard that it will be no later than the middle of next month.

Abolishing Taxes that Harm Agriculture

To Be Implemented Within One Week of Receipt of the Document

According to the New News Agency, the Ministry of Finance, based on the resolution of the Rural Rehabilitation Committee and the instructions of the Executive Yuan, issued a circular to the Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau yesterday, ordering it to investigate taxes and fees that hinder rural development and abolish them all within one week of receipt of the document. No delays shall be allowed under any pretext, and the names of the taxes and fees and the details of the abolition process shall be reported in detail for verification.

Shenxin Cotton Mill Resumes Work

Labor and Management Make Concessions

Successful Conclusion

The Shenxin Old and New Cotton Mills in Zhoujiaqiao, western Shanghai, caused repercussions due to the cancellation of worker bonuses. After repeated negotiations by the labor union failed, all 9,000 male and female workers went on strike at 3:00 PM on the 26th. Director Wen of the Public Security Bureau, the head of the Sixth District, and representatives from the City Party Headquarters, the Social Affairs Bureau, the General Labor Union, and the Tenth District Cotton Textile Labor Union, etc., repeatedly tried to mediate between labor and management. After two days, a settlement was reached on the afternoon of the day before yesterday (27th), and all workers expressed satisfaction and immediately resumed work. Thus, a storm came to an end.

Mediation Process: At around 10:00 AM the day before yesterday, Director Wen of the Public Security Bureau and District Head Tan of the Sixth District arrived at the factory one after another and tried to persuade the workers in each department and asked the factory to understand the workers' pain and allow concessions. At 3:00 PM, Lu Yinchu, a representative of the City Party Headquarters, Wang Xuanqing, a representative of the Social Affairs Bureau, and Fan Luquan, of the Tenth District Cotton Textile Labor Union, and others, mediated between the two sides again. At the same time, Luo Yifu, the engineer of the old factory, Lü Xingtang, the engineer of the new factory, and Tang Mengxiong, the engineer of the weaving room, tried their best to persuade the workers in each department. At 7:00 PM, a settlement was reached. The factory agreed to be considerate, and all workers expressed satisfaction.

Settlement Conditions: (1) The bonuses for May will be paid as usual. The bonuses for June and beyond will be decided based on the situation of each factory. (2) For the two days and two nights of the strike, a total of four workdays, labor and management will each sacrifice two workdays. The factory will pay wages for two workdays.

Resumption of Work: When the day shift workers left the factory and the night shift workers arrived, the workers expressed satisfaction. The day shift workers dispersed and the night shift workers entered in an orderly manner. Officer Wei of the Sixth District also led the police to protect and maintain order. At 7:45 PM, more than 2,000 night shift workers resumed work and started the machines to work as usual. At 5:00 AM yesterday, more than 3,000 day shift workers arrived at the factory for work. Because it was the Dragon Boat Festival according to the old calendar, not all of them arrived. It is estimated that all of them will be at work today.

Exporting Aged Silk with Government Subsidies

Ninety Percent of 20,000 Dan Exported

Deadline Is May 31st

The governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, in order to relieve the silk industry, issued 3 million yuan of short-term public bonds in 1932 and established the Committee for Promoting the Sale of Aged Factory Silk and the Committee for Organizing Aged Factory Silk and Aged Cocoons. For every dan of raw silk exported, a subsidy of 140 yuan is given. Now the two committees have been ordered to end at the end of this month and stop giving subsidies. The two committees have issued a notice as follows: "This committee is ordered to handle the export of subsidized aged factory silk. Now that 3 million yuan of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Silk Industry Short-Term Public Bonds of 1932 have been allocated, in addition to 200,000 yuan for the promotion fund, the remaining 2.8 million yuan is the export subsidy for 20,000 dan of aged silk. For every dan exported, 140 yuan of public bonds will be subsidized. As of today, 2,490,460 yuan of public bond certificates have been issued, leaving 309,540 yuan, which is only enough to subsidize the export of 2,211 dan of silk. If the total number of exports exceeds 20,000 dan by the end of May, this committee will submit a request to the Ministry of Industry, the Ministry of Finance, and the governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces for instructions. From now until May 31, the order in which subsidies are issued will be based on the export ship dates and the export certificate numbers of the Jianghai Customs. This is hereby notified. May 27."
