To Resist Japanese Goods and Promote Domestic Goods

A Letter from University Students to Businessmen

Without Developing National Industries, It Is Not Enough to Resist Strong Neighbors

Without Completely Banning Japanese Goods, It Is Not Enough to Develop National Industries

The Anti-Japanese Goods Movement Committee of the Shanghai University Student Union held its second meeting yesterday. Liu Xiru presided over the meeting, and Ren Jimo took the minutes. Important matters were discussed and resolved: (1) How to promote the "Thrift Movement Week"? It was resolved to have the Propaganda Group draft a plan and conduct it in various schools separately. (2) Date of the next meeting: It was resolved to hold it on June 3rd at 1:00 PM, convened by the person in charge of culture. (3) To resist Japanese goods and promote domestic goods, a letter to Shanghai businessmen was resolved to be amended and passed. The meeting adjourned. The letter to businessmen is recorded below: "Japanese Pirates Act Rampantly, Harming Our China. They have seized Manchuria and invaded North China. Their ambitions are rampant, and they want to encompass our country and enslave our Chinese people. For more than a year, their troops have seized land and attacked cities, advancing step by step. Our troops have fought hard and retreated step by step, forming the current situation of broken mountains and rivers and endangering the heartland. If we continue to passively retreat, what will be left of the nation? Retracting a hundred miles a day, how many times can our territory be cut? If our compatriots think about this and reflect on the dangers facing the country, the nation, and their families, they should tremble with cold. However, to merely sit and sigh today is not enough to save the chronic illness. To shout loudly is not enough to support the precarious situation. To merely blame the government is not enough to save the country. To merely rely on military force is not enough to resist Japan. The great power and the life force to resist the enemy still rely entirely on our people to rise up and save themselves. The rise and fall of the country is the responsibility of every man. The way to save the country is to do what we can. We cannot rush to the front and defend the country with weapons. We should also reflect on the pain and do our duty as citizens in the rear. What is the duty of the rear? What lies before us is to collect military supplies and provisions to maintain and solidify the front lines and to resist enemy goods to consolidate the foundation of the national economy. And to resist enemy goods and promote domestic goods is the most urgent task today. We know that for eighty years, due to the aggression of imperialists, China's rural economy has rapidly collapsed, and new industries have no way to develop, causing foreign goods to flood the market and local products to not leave the countryside. The dumping of Japanese goods is the biggest obstacle to domestic goods. Businessmen should know this even more clearly. Today's plan is that without developing national industries, it is not enough to resist strong neighbors, and without completely banning Japanese goods, it is not enough to develop national industries. International struggles in the twentieth century can be called economic struggles rather than military struggles. Our desire to resist Japanese goods and promote domestic goods is one reason. We all know that Japan has a small land area and a surplus of population. It regards our country's raw materials as the source of its industry and commerce and the Chinese market as the outlet for its life. Therefore, Japan fears our people's genuine resistance to goods more than the counterattack of the Northeast Volunteer Army. If the people can thoroughly realize the complete severance of relations with Japan, it will be enough to control Japan's lifeline, which is more effective than empty talk about resisting Japan. Our desire to resist Japanese goods and promote domestic goods is another reason. Since the Chinese resistance to Japanese goods movement began in 1907, there have been nine times. Every time after a resistance to goods, the sales of Japanese goods have increased instead. After the September 18th Incident, the whole country ran around and shouted, and the sound of resisting goods and checking goods filled the country. But our compatriots are forgetful. Before long, we heard that Japanese goods in Qingdao and Tianjin had increased greatly, and Japanese goods in Shanghai remained the same. This phenomenon cannot but be mourned by those who are close to us and cheered by those who are enemies. Businessmen, the danger of the country and the nation has reached this point. If the nation is subjugated, what will be left of our families? Although India is rich, it has become a British colony. Although Jews are good at managing wealth, they cannot avoid the sorrow of national subjugation. The dangerous situation of our country today is only a short distance from that. Today, all compatriots should use their conscience to love the country and save the country from their own position. If we can work together with one heart and cherish the determination to wipe out our humiliation, then the destruction of Qin by three households is not without reason. We have been greatly stimulated and vow to take the lead in saving the country and resisting foreign aggression. However, since we are not social producers, we can only make efforts to call and promote and prevent the best-selling Japanese goods in the Shanghai market. We rely entirely on the faithful execution of the business community. The situation is urgent and does not allow hesitation. If the country is destroyed and the family is destroyed, it is difficult to stand idly by. We dare to sincerely inform our businessmen to encourage each other to implement this purpose, build the foundation of the national economy, and seek the effectiveness of saving the country and wiping out humiliation. The country will be fortunate, and the compatriots will be fortunate. The Anti-Japanese Goods Movement Committee of the Shanghai University Student Union bows."

Overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia

Resolutely Oppose Postage Increase

Singapore Chinese Chamber of Commerce Telegram to Shanghai Chinese Associations

Expressing Opposition and Appealing for Vigorous Assistance

Regarding the issue of postage increases in Southeast Asia, it is now learned that the Ministry of Communications has decided to implement it from July 1st. A Far Eastern News Agency reporter, noting past opposition from overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia, visited Mr. Huang Jianzhong, a standing committee member of the Overseas Chinese United Association, yesterday afternoon. The reporter inquired about the association's attitude towards this issue and the recent expressions of overseas Chinese. Mr. Huang provided the following information:

Complicated Remittance Procedures

According to Mr. Huang, the authorities' stated reasons for the price increase are twofold: (1) the postal service's finances are affected by the gold standard in Southeast Asia; (2) the desire to suppress silver letter agencies and unify the postal system. However, the suffering of the general Chinese working class in Southeast Asia must be understood and forgiven by both the public and the government. Most of these workers are illiterate laborers with meager incomes. When they occasionally have a dozen or so yuan, they must remit it home to support their families. If they remit through the post office, they must first pay someone to write a letter, then go to the post office to pay the remittance fee, registration fee, and other fees. Before the money and letter are even sent, they have already spent about two yuan. After the money and letter arrive, the postman delivering it to the countryside demands another four or five jiao. In total, remitting a dozen or so yuan requires spending three yuan. How can the general working class afford this? Therefore, silver letter agencies have naturally emerged.

Letter Agencies are Very Convenient

Silver letter agencies are a type of commercial organization that specializes in profiting from fluctuations in silver prices. Those remitting money and letters only need to go to a silver letter agency, state where to remit, and how much silver to remit. The silver letter agency will write the letter for free and does not require any remittance fee. After the letter arrives at its destination, the agency can also write a reply for the recipient, without requiring any further fees. In total, remitting ten yuan only costs five fen in postage. This is the convenience of silver letter agencies, which is why they are popular with the general public. Silver letter agencies send letters in bundles of one hundred, each bundle with five fen in postage. If the price increases, each bundle would require twelve yuan, which would naturally be opposed by the general overseas Chinese.

Our Association's Stance

The postage increase in Southeast Asia was originally intended to be implemented on April 1st. Due to strong opposition, it was postponed to May 1st. On May 1st, the Ministry of Communications indicated a further postponement. Recently, our association sent representatives to Beijing to investigate. It was learned that the Ministry of Communications had decided to announce the implementation from July 1st. We immediately telegraphed various Chinese organizations in Southeast Asia and sent representatives to Xiamen, Shantou, and other places to report to the local guilds of silver letter agencies. As a Chinese organization, our association should naturally seek the welfare of overseas Chinese. Regarding the postage increase in Southeast Asia, we will adopt a unified stance with overseas Chinese organizations and consistently express our opposition.

Overseas Chinese Unanimously Oppose

Since receiving our association's report, Chinese organizations at home and abroad have sent letters and telegrams to our association, expressing their resolute opposition and appealing for assistance. We recently received a telegram from the Singapore Chinese Chamber of Commerce. Immediately, the telegram was retrieved and shown to the reporter, and is recorded as follows: (The first part omitted) "Your telegram of the fifth (May) received. If postage increases, the burden on overseas Chinese will increase, and the livelihoods of their families will be difficult to support. We have telegraphed the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission and the Ministry of Communications, requesting consideration of the difficulties faced by overseas Chinese and approval to postpone the increase. Your association's concern for fellow overseas Chinese and call for vigorous assistance is greatly appreciated."

Lian An Company's Taizhou Steamer

Robbed by Pirates Outside Haimen

Three Killed, Including a Water Police Officer; Three Passengers Injured

Entire Ship Looted; Two People Kidnapped Before Departure

Heavy Losses; Company Sends Telegram Demanding Strict Capture of Pirates

The Taizhou steamer, owned by the Taizhou Xinji Shipping Bureau and operated by Lian An Navigation Company on the Wenzhou-Taizhou route, was scheduled to sail from Haimen to Shanghai on the evening of the 24th of this month. Outside Haimen, in the waters of Nanbei Ze, it was robbed by pirates. Two water police officers and one female passenger were killed, two passengers and one cabin boy were injured, and two passengers were kidnapped. The losses amounted to over 20,000 yuan. The details are as follows:

Pirates Infiltrated

Lian An Company owns six steamships: Zhoushan, Daxing, Chuanshan, Yili, Dahua, and Taizhou, which operate between Shanghai, Dinghai, Haimen, and Shipu. The Taizhou steamer, with a tonnage of 1,200 tons, is owned by the Taizhou Shipping Company. On Wednesday, the 24th of this month, at 6:00 PM, it set sail from Haimen fully loaded with passengers and cargo, bound for Shanghai. Eleven pirates had infiltrated among the passengers. At 8:00 PM, when the ship reached the waters of Nanbei Ze outside Haimen, fifteen li from Haimen, the infiltrated pirates, each armed with guns, first ordered the captain, Mr. Xu, and the chief mate to steer the ship between Langqi Mountain and Dachen Mountain.

Passengers Killed and Injured

Two armed water police officers from the Dinghai Water Police Bureau were traveling to Haimen on official business and were on the Taizhou steamer returning to Dinghai. The infiltrated pirates, fearing resistance from the water police, took them by surprise and fired wildly. The water police officers were immediately killed. At the same time, three passengers and one cabin boy were wounded by stray bullets. Among the passengers, a thirteen-year-old girl from Haimen returning to Shipu was seriously injured and died immediately. The ship fell into chaos, and the pirates began to loot.

Everything Looted

The Taizhou steamer was forced by the pirates to sail to the waters between Langqi Mountain and Dachen Mountain, a den of thieves. The pirates then ordered the ship to anchor. More than ten pirate ships, all carrying pirates, swarmed aboard and looted at will, numerous times. Passengers and crew members had their personal belongings, clothing, and silver dollars stolen, down to their shoes and socks. Passengers who refused to obey were beaten. The pirates were extremely brutal.

People Kidnapped Before Departure

The pirates looted the steamer for as long as twenty-four hours. After everything of value had been taken, the crew and passengers, wearing only single layers of clothing and barefoot, were sent to small boats, to be returned to the pirates' den, between Langqi Mountain and Dachen Mountain. Before leaving, the pirates kidnapped two passengers. After boarding the small boats, one of the kidnapped passengers, surnamed Wang, was released. At 7:00 PM on the 25th, the Taizhou steamer finally escaped and immediately sailed back to Haimen.

Escaped and Returned

Upon returning to Haimen, the Taizhou steamer immediately sent the three injured passengers and cabin boy to the Haimen Hospital for treatment. Fortunately, their injuries were minor and not life-threatening. The bodies of the two water police officers and the female passenger who were killed were immediately reported, inspected, and collected. At the same time, the Taizhou Xinji Shipping Bureau's headquarters in Haimen was notified, and telegrams were sent to Dinghai, Shipu, and the local military and police authorities, demanding the strict capture of the pirates. After receiving the report, Zhu Daoji, a director of the headquarters, rushed back to Haimen from Dinghai to handle the matter and telegraphed the Lian An Company in Shanghai.

Heavy Losses

After the looting, the Taizhou steamer's accounting office reported the loss of 875.50 yuan in water transport fees and 400 yuan in passenger tickets. Over thirty merchants traveling from Haimen to Shanghai to purchase goods suffered losses of over 20,000 yuan. The losses of personal belongings, clothing, and silver dollars of the crew and passengers were impossible to calculate at the time. The Lian An Company's Zhoushan steamer arrived in Shanghai from Haimen yesterday. The captain reported the details of the Taizhou robbery.

Strict Capture of Pirates

A reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency interviewed a clerk from the Taizhou Shipping Company and crew members from the Zhoushan steamer yesterday. They said that the Taizhou steamer was unfortunately robbed by pirates, resulting in heavy losses. The Haimen headquarters has sent a telegram demanding the strict capture of the pirates. The Taizhou steamer is scheduled to sail from Haimen to Shanghai on the 31st of this month and arrive in Shanghai on the 2nd of next month.

Page 9

Shortening Travel Time on Two Railway Lines

Train Numbers and Travel Times Changed

Approved by the Ministry of Railways, Effective June 1st

China Internal News Agency reports that the Traffic Department of the Joint Management Bureau of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways, due to orders from the Bureau to shorten the travel time of express trains and in accordance with the locomotive department's regulations on the running times of various trains, has compiled the second edition of the timetable, which has been approved by the Ministry of Railways and will be implemented from June 1st of this year. All inbound trains in the table will be renumbered with even numbers, and outbound trains will be renumbered with odd numbers, to conform to the numbering methods of other state-owned railway trains and demonstrate uniformity. The revised times for each line are detailed below:

Beijing-Shanghai Line

Shortening the Travel Time of Express Trains

The newly ordered special express trains, except for the fifth and sixth night special express trains, the first and fourth special express trains (i.e., the existing second and third special express trains) have had their travel times reduced to six hours and fifty minutes. Each train is limited to twelve carriages and is hauled by Pacific locomotives. The travel times of the 302nd and 301st inbound and outbound Shanghai-Beijing through express trains have also been reduced to seven hours and forty minutes and seven hours respectively. The travel time of the second inbound express train on this line has also been reduced to seven hours.

Adding Shanghai-Beijing Through Express Train

Adding the 302nd inbound Shanghai-Beijing through express train. After consultation with the Tianjin-Pukou Railway authorities, it will depart from the North Shanghai Station at 1:00 AM daily and arrive in Beijing at 8:40 AM. As the inbound night express train on that line departs earlier, and the Tianjin-Pukou Railway authorities do not want through passengers to wait too long in Pukou, the departure and arrival times of this train could not be advanced further. In the future, all carriages will use the through trains organized by the various lines. However, before the ferry service between Beijing and Pukou begins, the line plans to temporarily use its own carriages, including eight first-class and second-class passenger carriages each, four third-class passenger carriages, two baggage-mail carriages, and other mail and parcel carriages, and only sell tickets for this line. Until the ferry service between Beijing and Pukou is established, this through train will use the carriages of the existing fourth express train on this line. The departure time, after consultation with the Tianjin-Pukou authorities, is scheduled to be 5:25 PM from Beijing, arriving at the North Shanghai Station at 0:25 AM the next day. At the same time, it is also limited to only selling tickets for this line. (Note) Before the Tianjin-Pukou Railway timetable is completely revised, all through passengers between Shanghai and Beijing will still be transported by the first and fourth trains (i.e., the existing second and third trains).

Canceling the Midday Train from Shanghai to Beijing

To save locomotive power, the line plans to cancel the existing 11th inbound midday express train from Shanghai to Beijing. The saved locomotives will be used to run the newly added 302nd inbound Shanghai-Beijing through express train. The cancellation of the midday express train will not cause inconvenience to passengers traveling between Shanghai and Beijing. According to the current outbound timetable, the midday express train makes more stops in the Shanghai to Zhenjiang section. After Zhenjiang, it travels directly to Nanjing without stopping along the way. Passengers traveling from Shanghai to Beijing can take the 2nd inbound (i.e., the current 1st train) Shanghai-Beijing through express train, which departs from North Shanghai at 3:10 PM. Because the travel time of the express train has been shortened, the arrival time in Beijing is almost the same as the original midday express train.

Extending the Shanghai-Changzhou Service to Zhenjiang

After the cancellation of the 11th inbound midday express train from Shanghai to Beijing, to compensate for the convenience of passengers at stations in the Shanghai to Zhenjiang section, it has been decided to extend the Shanghai-Changzhou service to Zhenjiang, changing it to the Shanghai-Zhenjiang service. This service is scheduled to depart from North Shanghai Station at 12:15 PM and arrive at Zhenjiang Station at 8:10 PM. In this case, passengers on the existing 11th express train can take this service. Although the midday express train is canceled, it will not be affected. The existing 22nd outbound Changzhou-Shanghai service will be changed to the 21st outbound Zhenjiang-Shanghai service, departing from Zhenjiang Station. The purpose is to reduce congestion on the 7th outbound Beijing-Shanghai early express train (i.e., the current 10th train). It is scheduled to depart from Zhenjiang Station at 7:05 AM and arrive at North Shanghai Station at 3:00 PM. (Note) The above-mentioned Zhenjiang-Shanghai service is a measure to consider the convenience of passengers. However, before the facilities at Zhenjiang Station are completed, the locomotives used for the Zhenjiang-Shanghai service must travel from Changzhou. After the locomotives for the Shanghai-Zhenjiang service arrive in Zhenjiang, they must return to Changzhou. During these return trips, the locomotives will inevitably travel in reverse, so it must be handled according to regulations, limiting the speed to 40 kilometers per hour. The Traffic Department is currently seeking instructions from the Administration on this point. The existing 4th outbound Beijing-Shanghai express train will be changed to the 301st through train in the future. Its departure time from Beijing must be delayed to 5:25 PM. To facilitate passengers traveling from Beijing to stations in the Wuxi section, it is planned to advance the existing Beijing-Wuxi service to 2:00 PM, departing from Beijing. Passengers traveling from Beijing to stations in the Zhenjiang section, if they feel that the departure time from Beijing is too early, can take the recently added 25th outbound (i.e., the current 28th train) Beijing-Zhenjiang service.

Beijing-Zhenjiang Service Awaiting Implementation

The Railway Administration believes that Nanjing is the capital and Zhenjiang is the provincial capital. Although the distance is short, passenger traffic is frequent. Therefore, it has decided to add the 26th inbound and 25th outbound Zhenjiang-Beijing services to facilitate passengers. However, they will only be launched after the necessary facilities at Zhenjiang Station are completed.

Inbound Express Train Departure Delayed

The current 3rd special express train and the current 7th early express train are very close in time on the route, making overtaking possible. In the future, the travel time of the special express train must be shortened. To avoid overtaking on the route, it is planned to change the departure time of the 4th express train from North Shanghai Station to 10:00 AM daily, the same as the departure time of the 1st train from Beijing.

One Night Express Train in Each Direction

It has been decided that night express trains will only run one train in each direction. The Chief of the Locomotive Department has agreed to save locomotive power and facilitate train operation. The Chief of the Locomotive Department has also stated that there are no problems with heating equipment for the autumn and winter seasons.

Songhu Line

Songhu Line Adds Twelve Services

The Songhu Branch Line currently has a total of 28 services in both directions. In recent months, passenger traffic on the line has been improving daily. To facilitate travel, the number of services in the newly ordered timetable is planned to increase to a total of 40 in both directions. Two steam carriages and two ordinary locomotives hauling passenger carriages will be used in rotation. One of the two steam carriages is planned to be used as a backup. After this revision, it is expected that travel on the line will be greatly facilitated. The running times of freight trains have also been included in accordance with the Ministry's orders, with four services in each direction.

Shanghai-Hangzhou Line

Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Line Also Changed

The Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Line has also been changed. The results of the investigation are as follows: (1) The existing 31st and 32nd inbound and outbound Shanghai-Beijing through express trains have been changed to the 2nd inbound and 1st outbound Shanghai-Beijing through express trains, consistent with the corresponding trains on the Beijing-Shanghai Line. (2) The departure time of the 37th outbound (i.e., the current 40th) third and fourth-class slow train from North Shanghai Station is planned to be advanced to 9:50 AM to avoid conflicting with the departure time of the 4th inbound (i.e., the current 3rd) train on the Beijing-Shanghai Line from North Shanghai Station. (3) The planned Huzhou-Shanghai service, due to a shortage of locomotives in the Locomotive Department, has not been restored. The existing 35th and 36th Shanghai-Huzhou express trains have the characteristics of the Huzhou-Shanghai service in the Huzhou-Shanghai section. Therefore, there is no great inconvenience in terms of travel. (4) The running times of other trains are roughly the same as the existing timetable, except for slight changes in the stops.

Taxation Administration Changes Beer Tax Rate

Changed to Specific Tax

Effective the 15th of Next Month

The General Affairs Department of the Ministry of Finance in this city believes that since the domestic beer manufacturing industry switched to on-site taxation in 1931, tax revenues have improved. The current tax rate is 20% ad valorem, assessed on the market price when the factory is opened. This has been in effect for a long time, but market prices fluctuate constantly, leading to many discrepancies in practice. Moreover, ad valorem pricing involves complicated procedures, and the tax amount is not always fair. To standardize taxation, the tax rate for domestically produced beer will be changed to a specific tax. Regardless of the selling price, a box of 48 large bottles (quart bottles) or 72 small bottles (pint bottles) will be taxed at 2.60 yuan. Barrel or cask beer will be taxed at 7 fen per liter of net capacity. The outside of barrels or casks should be marked with the net liters for verification. The specific tax rate will be implemented nationwide from June 15th of this year to ensure standardization.

Cancellation of Land Tax for Beihui Section of County Road

The Beihui section of the Songhu Road on the Shanghai side used land for road construction. The land prices have already been paid separately. The county government believes that the land tax for these road lands should be canceled. After verification, a list was submitted to the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance for approval. The Department approved the cancellation, and the county government has ordered the Land Tax Collection Office to comply.

Xu Xueyu

Discusses Reasons for Telephone Price Increase

City Chamber of Commerce to Meet Today

Since the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications increased prices, various trade associations have opposed it. The City Chamber of Commerce plans to send representatives to the Telephone Bureau to negotiate a temporary suspension of charges. Yesterday, according to an interview with Xu Xueyu, the director of the Telephone Bureau, the City Chamber of Commerce has sent a letter informing them of their plan to send representatives to the Bureau to negotiate. He has replied, inviting them to meet at the Bureau on Monday (today) morning to explain everything. As for the Bureau's financial situation, before the conversion to automatic machinery, strict austerity measures were taken to barely balance income and expenses. After the conversion, the Bureau must pay US$4,000 per month in debt, equivalent to about 20,000 yuan. There are currently only 2,530 subscribers, of which 200 have not been converted to automatic machinery and are still charged at the old rate. The newly set rates are seven yuan for residential lines and ten yuan for business lines, with a monthly income of about 21,000 yuan, which barely covers the Bureau's expenses. The US$4,000 debt and the cost of repairs and supplies still need to be raised. As for the cancellation of the concession telephone fee, the Bureau consulted with the concession company on the method of canceling the five-fen call fee when the automatic exchange was opened. The company did not agree due to excessive losses. The Bureau is still in consultation with the company to achieve this goal.

Anhui Rice Merchant Chen Dajiang Missing

Please Anhui Compatriots Association Help Investigate

Chen Dajiang, a member of the Anhui Rice Merchants Association in Shanghai, is a rice merchant. The Association recently reorganized its affairs and invited all members to gather at the Gongdelin on Parker Road on the 22nd of this month. Chen also attended. Unexpectedly, Chen disappeared the next day. He was searched everywhere, but there was no news. The Association has published advertisements in various newspapers to find him and has reported the case to the Bazha Patrol Room and the Zhabei Public Security Bureau. It has been a week, but there is still no news. The Association has sent a letter to the Anhui Compatriots Association in Shanghai requesting assistance in the investigation. The letter states: "Dear Sirs, Chen Dajiang, a rice merchant stationed in Shanghai at the Xiechangde Rice Mill on the north bank of the New Garbage Bridge, is a member of the Executive Committee of the Association. On the afternoon of the 22nd of this month, he went to Gongdelin at 6:00 PM for the Association's dinner appointment. Chen left alone at 8:15 PM and has not returned to the factory since. His whereabouts are unknown. In addition to publishing advertisements to find him and reporting the case to the patrol room for investigation, we are sending this letter to your Association, requesting that you distribute letters to various agencies for a thorough investigation, in order to uncover the truth. We have always admired your Association's concern for our hometown, and we are sure you will grant our request. A resume of Chen Dajiang is attached as follows: Chen Dajiang, 55 years old, from Hanshan County, Anhui Province, is over five feet tall, with a long face, a mustache, and a flat-top haircut. He is wearing a dark blue gabardine long gown. He has been transporting and selling Anhui rice in Shanghai for more than ten years." The Compatriots Association, based on the situation, has sent letters to the agencies, requesting an investigation.

China Agricultural and Industrial Bank Shareholders' General Meeting

On the afternoon of the 28th of this month at 2:00 PM, the China Agricultural and Industrial Bank held its sixth shareholders' general meeting at the bank's headquarters at the intersection of Second Ma Road and Henan Road. The shareholders present included Cai Zimin, Zhang Jingjiang, Li Shizeng, Fang Yaoting, Song Ziliang, Zhou Zuomin, Lu Hanyun, Wang Ganfeng, Wu Zhenxiu, Feng Youwei, Wei Bocong, Qi Zhi, Wang Guohua, Cheng Zhenji, Nie Guoliang, Hu Pinsan, and over one hundred others. Chairman of the Board Li Yuying was elected as the chairman of the meeting. First, the chairman delivered the opening address, stating that during the past year, the national crisis has become more urgent and commerce has declined, creating a special difficulty for the financial sector. The bank's main goal is to consolidate its foundation and preserve its strength. All operations are viewed in terms of their potential for development, and attention is paid to rural economic issues in the spirit of its name. Although the past year has been extremely difficult, all operations have developed, and the profits are better than last year. This is comforting to the shareholders. The operating situation will be reported in detail by the general manager and need not be repeated here. One matter is important to our bank and should be reported to everyone. General Manager Yao Kui has resigned from his positions as general manager and director due to illness. His intention is firm. The fourth meeting of the third board of directors approved his resignation from the position of general manager, but he will remain as a director. Associate Manager Qi Zhi was appointed as general manager and will also serve as the manager of the Shanghai branch. The center of office operations at the general office will be shifted from the general manager system to the board of directors system. The chairman of the board, standing directors, and general manager will jointly be responsible for the affairs. Since I have been serving as chairman of the board, I have made few contributions to the bank's affairs. I am not a banking expert and feel deeply ashamed. I went abroad for eight months last year. Mr. Zhou Zuomin served as my proxy and made many contributions to the bank's affairs. This term of the board of directors, I will be going to Europe again and have suggested that Mr. Zhang Gongquan serve as acting chairman of the board. In the future, our bank will have a famous figure in the financial sector to preside over the bank's affairs, which will surely lead to daily progress. This is what I am most pleased about. Then, he reported the number of shares present, reported on the operating situation of the previous year and the settlement situation. The total number of accounts and deposits, the total number of issuances, and the number of loans and other operations all increased compared to 1931. Then, he reported on the profit distribution plan for the previous year and the method of changing the resolution to amend the charter of the previous year. Next, the supervisors were re-elected. The chairman appointed Wu Zhenxiu, Lu Hanyun, Xia Weiru, and Cheng Zhenji as ballot counters. Zhang Renjie, Wang Junyi, Xia Weiru, Wu Zhenxiu, and Nie Guoliang were elected as supervisors, and Zhu Junyong, Cai Yuankun, and Peng Jiqun were elected as alternate supervisors. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM. The shareholders had refreshments at will, and the meeting dispersed at 6:00 PM.

Nitric Sulfur Bureau Seizes Large Quantities of Illegally Stored Goods

The Nitric Sulfur Branch Bureau of the Jiangsu Provincial Treasury Department in Shanghai has recently learned that pharmacies in the French Concession are secretly selling illegally stored nitric sulfur, which violates the ban. The Bureau, being responsible for this matter, dispatched inspectors to investigate and found that Songbaiyuan, Wanxiangchun, and other stores had illegally stored nitric sulfur and sulfur. They had no passports or waybills. After review by Bureau Chief Chen Peng, it was deemed that they had clearly violated criminal law and could not be excused. Songbaiyuan and Wanxiangchun have been transferred to the Shanghai Second Special District Court for the crime under Article 201 to serve as a warning. The other stores will also be transferred for legal proceedings as soon as the investigation is verified.

It is widely known that the success or failure of industry depends on chemistry as its foundation. All industries are like this. Villagers Killed by Robbers While Apprehending Them

In the Xin Kai He Zhai village of Baoshan County, north of Wusong, more than ten robbers suddenly came to the house of a local resident, Ding Mao, at about 10 PM the other night. They intimidated them with guns and robbed them of silver, money, and jewelry worth about 800 taels of silver, then fled with loud shouts. When nearby neighbors heard the noise, they gathered dozens of people to pursue and capture them. Seeing the situation was not good, the robbers fired more than ten shots. The villagers all ducked to the ground when they heard the gunshots. Among them, Qian Zhen, who was fifty-eight years old, volunteered and continued to chase forward. As a result, he was shot three times. Although he was injured and fell to the ground, he managed to crawl back home, but died of his injuries yesterday morning. The villagers have reported the incident to the Baoshan County government for verification.

Entertainment

"Spring Water, Love Waves" Premieres at the New Light Theater Today The latest production of the Star Film Company, "Spring Water, Love Waves," is a masterpiece directed by the famous director Zheng Zhengqiu after "The Flower of Freedom." The script is adapted from Pan Fuliang's novel "Saoxing." The plot is tactful, and the meaning is cautionary. The content tells the story of a playboy who returns from studying abroad. Driven by lust, he has an affair with a maid in his house. Then he enters the officialdom and falls in love with a socialite and a politician's daughter one after another, leaving the maid behind. In the end, this playboy is abandoned by both lovers and reflects on his behavior. When he returns to the maid, she has suffered a lot but resolutely refuses. She has dedicated herself to society and is working hard for social causes. The protagonist, Hu Die, plays the maid, Sun Min plays the playboy, Hu Ping plays the socialite, and Yan Yuexian plays the politician's daughter. They can all display their strengths and perform to their heart's content. The sets and photography of the whole film are excellent, and it is truly a valuable work. It has been scheduled to premiere at the New Light Theater on Ningbo Road today (the 27th).

Star Dance School Holds Tea Dance The Star Dance School at 602 Xiafei Road in this city is scheduled to hold a tea dance party today, Saturday, starting at 5 pm. A grand occasion is expected at that time.

Tragic Incident at Xiang Stage on Tianbao Road, Zhabei Yesterday

More than Twenty People Trampled to Death or Injured

Dragon Boat Festival Performance of "Legend of the White Snake"

Refinery Suddenly Catches Fire

Spectators Flee in Panic

Police Suppress and Hospitals Treat the Wounded

Yesterday afternoon, at about 1:50 PM, a tragic incident occurred at the Xiang Stage on Tianbao Road, Zhabei, with more than twenty people killed or injured. The details are recorded below.

Watching a Play on the Dragon Boat Festival The Xiang Stage is located at the intersection of Tianbao Road and Xiangyan Bridge in Zhabei, specializing in performing Huaiyang opera. Therefore, the people who come to enjoy the opera on weekdays are mostly residents of Jiangsu and Anhui. The ticket prices are very cheap, so people flock to it, and the business is quite good. Yesterday was the abolished lunar Dragon Boat Festival, and all factories and other places were closed for the holiday. The workers nearby took this opportunity to go out for leisure. At the same time, the Xiang Stage was performing the timely play "Legend of the White Snake." As a result, a group of nearby residents, both old and young, went to watch the play. The upper and lower floors were immediately full.

False Rumor of Electrocution Unexpectedly, not long after the performance started, a fire suddenly broke out in the machine room of the China Refining Company at No. 10 Hengxingfang, Zhangjia Lane, at the end of Ping Road behind the stage. The nearby residents were panicked. At the same time, the police on duty went out to blow whistles to warn the public. The sound was heard inside the theater. One or two well-meaning spectators rushed out to investigate. They saw white smoke billowing outside the door and thought that there was an electrocution in the theater. They hurriedly went inside to call out their companions. When other spectators saw the panicked state of these people, they asked what was happening. Under the false rumor,

Inauguration Ceremony of the Sujia Highway

丨Held in Suzhou on June 19丨

Dong Xiujia, the director of Jiangsu Construction, in order to strive for the transportation between Suzhou and Jiaxing and to revitalize the market in Jiaxing, once consulted with the Zhejiang Construction authorities on the planning of the Sujia Highway. The construction departments of the two provinces also sent special commissioners to jointly inspect and build the route and carry out the steps. It was decided that the route would start from Suzhou, pass through Beiju, Pingwang, Wangjiangjing, and other places, and go directly to Jiaxing in Zhejiang. The required funds were jointly borne by the construction departments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang. This project, which is 77.7 kilometers long, started construction in 1921. According to the original plan, it could be completed by June last year. However, since the January 28th Shanghai War, the construction project was suspended, and the road that had already taken shape was damaged by Japanese aircraft bombing, causing particularly severe damage. Last year, when Finance Minister Song Ziwen convened the Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui Three Provinces Highway Conference in Nanjing, he personally instructed the construction directors of Jiangsu and Zhejiang to quickly complete the Sujia Highway to facilitate transportation between the two provinces. The original route was re-planned and changed to start from Suzhou, passing through Pingwang, Jingduan City, Shengze, Wangjiangjing, and then to Jiaxing, and construction was continued. According to reconnaissance reports, the project has now completed 80% of the work. A total of 18 bridges and 8 culverts have been completed. It is expected that the entire project will be completed within the next week or so. The Sujia Highway Engineering Office will also be abolished to close the project. It is also heard that the authorities of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces have decided to hold an inauguration ceremony in Suzhou on June 18. At that time, groups from Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces will be invited to send representatives to set off by car to inspect the entire highway project.

Spreading throughout the Theater, the spectators on the upper floor also rushed to leave their seats and escape towards the stairs.

Crowded Stairs Unfortunately, the stairs were narrow and there were too many people. At the same time, the entrance was blocked by the spectators downstairs, making it impossible to escape. However, those behind continued to push forward. As a result, more than twenty people standing on the steps fell down the stairs, but those behind were still trying their best to push forward. Thus, more than twenty people who fell on the steps were trampled on by the crowd. The screams were unbearable to hear. After receiving the report, the third squadron of the fifth district urgently dispatched all the police to suppress the crowd and tried their best to disperse them. At the same time, they cooperated with the fire brigade to put out the fire in the refinery company.

Names of the Seriously Injured In about half an hour, the fire was completely extinguished. At the same time, the police officers at the Xiang Stage carried out the injured separately. Among them, twelve had been trampled to death. They were sent to Tongren and Guangren hospitals in fire trucks. There were five injured males: (1) Yin A Gen, 32 years old, from Ningbo, left hand, (2) Wu Jinwei, 15 years old, from Jiangbei, head, (3) Zhang Su, 26 years old, from Jiangbei, abdomen, (4) Yuan Zhengjin, 14 years old, from Jiangbei, brain, (5) Unnamed, about 20 years old, very slight abdominal injury. There were four females, among whom, apart from one woman, the remaining three were all girls. Currently, there are seven people with minor injuries in Guangren Hospital, namely: Li Dekui, 14 years old, from Jiangbei, Wei Gentaozi, 10 years old, from Jiangbei, Zhang Guiyao, 11 years old, from Shaoxing, Zhang Quanfu, 15 years old, from Shaoxing, Shi Fumin, 14 years old, from Haimen, Qian Cuxian, 21 years old, from Ningbo, and Zhang Kuanquan, 11 years old, from Hangzhou. They are currently being treated at Tongren Hospital.

Twelve Dead A total of twelve people were trampled to death by the crowd, all with blood on their faces. The scene was too horrible to bear. Currently, the corpses have been carried to the open space there by the third squadron of the fifth district, and the local court has been requested to send personnel to verify the deaths. At the same time, an investigation into the families of the deceased will be conducted. By 9 PM, all of the deceased had been identified by their families. Among them, eight were males: Han Gendi, 12 years old, and Han Liuzhizi, 5 years old, both from Funing, Chen Jinsong, 17 years old, from Nanxiang, Yin Yunde, 8 years old, from Ningbo, Zhao Xiaosanzi, 16 years old, and Zhao Xiaowuzi, 13 years old, both from Baoying, Xu Miaogen, 7 years old, from Ningbo, and one unidentified male corpse. Currently, no family members have come to identify it. There were four females: Guo Wangshi, 59 years old, from Nanjing, Wang Damao, 14 years old, from Si Tang, Pan Zhaodi, 13 years old, and Pan Gendi, 9 years old, all from Tianjin. In total, there were 28 people killed or injured. At the same time, after the incident occurred, the responsible sub-precinct ordered the Xiang Stage to temporarily suspend business.

On the Shanghai-Hangzhou Road, a Car Crashes into the Corner of a House

One Killed, Four Injured

The Driver Flees

Since the opening of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway, merchants and businessmen in Shanghai often take cars from Shanghai to Hangzhou for sightseeing. As a result, cars come and go endlessly on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Road, and accidents often occur. The day before yesterday afternoon, a car with license plate number 5458 from the Shanghai Public Works Bureau and license plate number 8396 from the Concession, owned by a certain Mr. Shuang, was carrying four passengers and was returning to Shanghai from Hangzhou. When the car drove to the Jinshanwei Station area of Fengxian County, the driver accidentally veered the car, causing the front of the car to crash into the corner of the station, injuring five villagers. One of them, Chen Yinquan, died instantly due to injuries to vital areas. The station staff detained the car and summoned the police to take the four passengers in the car, along with the car, to the Public Security Bureau for investigation. The four injured villagers were put on a public bus and taken to Shanghai for hospital treatment. The driver of the car, seeing that an accident had occurred, took advantage of the crowd's commotion and fled without a trace. The body of the villager Chen Yinquan who was killed was reported by the local bailiff to the Fengxian County Government for verification.

A Gruesomely Murdered Male Corpse Discovered on Beile Road in the Dim Light of Night

A Total of Thirty-One Knife and Axe Wounds All Over the Body

No Family Members Found, Awaiting Hospital Verification Today

At 2:15 AM yesterday, two Chinese detectives, No. 533 and No. 700, from the Lou Ka Wan Central Police Station in the French Concession, were patrolling the south side of the road about ten zhang west of the western end of Beile Road, Kang Ti Road, in front of the gate of No. 331. They discovered an unidentified man lying face up on the sidewalk, head facing east and feet facing west. They called out to him, but he did not respond. They kicked him, but he did not move. When they leaned down to inspect, he had already died. His face was covered in blood, and he had been hacked to death with a knife. They moved the corpse to that location. One detective watched over the corpse, while the other rushed back to the Central Police Station to report. The head detective sent investigators to inspect the scene. It was found that the corpse was short in stature, wearing a striped Yuan Se serge long gown, with a vest underneath, Western-style single trousers, and small round-toed serge shoes, with black rubber galoshes on the outside. Upon detailed inspection, the corpse had a total of twenty-two or three large wounds from being hacked, and seven or eight small wounds from being stabbed with a knife, from head to toe and on both arms. The left leg was broken and stacked on top of the right leg. The clothes were completely torn. The corpse had red and green tattoos on both arms, and a strongman dancing with immortals carrying flowers tattooed on its chest. Two gold teeth were inlaid in the upper part of the mouth. The scene was too horrible to bear. Most of the bloodstains on the ground had been washed away by the rain, and the remaining bloodstains were already blurred. According to the detectives' speculation, the deceased was likely lured to the location and hacked to death. A murder weapon, an axe, was found about one storefront to the west of the location where the corpse was found. The detective took it back to the police station and reported to the head detective, who notified the Fuyuan branch, ordering the undertaker to go to the autopsy room to transport the corpse. No family members were found. The Second Special District Court will be requested to send personnel to verify the corpse today. At the same time, Western detective Fu Yu notified detectives in the Western section, both Chinese and Western, to pay attention to strictly apprehending the murderer and bringing him to justice.

Mr. Zhang Commits Suicide by Drowning Out of Indignation at National Affairs

Fifty-Word Suicide Note

Warned by the Authorities

The China Merchants Bureau's Xin Jiangtian (Shanghai-Ningbo route) ship, which was fully loaded with passengers, departed from Shanghai on the afternoon of the 24th and arrived at the mouth of Zhenhai at 4:30 AM the next morning, the 25th, about to enter the port. A third-class passenger surnamed Zhang, 22 years old, from Hunan, who was an employee of a foreign company in Shanghai, felt disgusted and harbored the thought of ending his life. He sneaked to the deck and jumped into the sea, taking advantage of the unpreparedness of others. The sailors on the ship noticed and stopped the ship to rescue him. However, the sky was not yet bright, and the waves were rough. They watched as the young man was swept away by the huge waves, and there was no way to save him. Afterwards, the steward of the ship found a suicide note in his berth, which read: "Japanese bandits are invading our territory, and the state affairs are deteriorating. Rather than becoming a subjugated slave in the future, why not throw myself into the Qing stream now and end this broken body. I hope that all the honorable gentlemen will quickly rise up and rejuvenate the country, and save the people, which is also to save the country." It was signed with the surname Zhang.

Lost Girl Picked Up

A police officer of the second squadron of the Public Security Bureau found a lost girl, Zhang Xiaoer, near the Sanwan Factory in Lujiazai, Pudong, the day before yesterday evening and sent her to the third district. According to Zhang, she is 15 years old and from Taixing. She lost her mother at a young age. Last year, she came to Shanghai with her father and was sent to work at the Gongda Cotton Mill. Recently, the factory has been reducing female workers due to poor business. I was also laid off this time and have no place to live. I wanted to go back to my hometown, but I am not familiar with the route, which led to me getting lost. Since the chief district could not find any family to claim her, she was sent to the General Bureau for relief yesterday.

American Silver Prices Soar

Reuters, New York, 27th: Deferred silver prices have soared due to government legislation to abolish the gold standard, and speculators are buying heavily. Today's opening price was 100 to 160 points higher than Friday's closing price. It then fell slightly, and then rose slightly again. The closing price was 90 to 105 points higher than the previous day's closing price. The volume traded was 5.15 million ounces. Today's nearby listing price was one cent higher than one day, at 3.425 cents. The actual transaction price was 3.47/8 cents, which is 1.25 cents higher than the previous day.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the sky was cloudy in Shandong, with wind coming from the east. The middle and lower reaches of the Yangtze River had north to northeast winds, with fog in the morning. In the area from the Ma'an Islands to the coast, the sky was overcast with rain or heavy fog, and the northeast wind was strong and gusty. There was a cyclone rainstorm around the Ryukyu Islands, caused by a low pressure system passing through and moving east or east-northeast. Also, within the 24 hours before 3 PM yesterday, the temperature in the city was a high of 76.5 and a low of 58.1. On the same day last year, the high was 90.5 and the low was 65.7.

He Fangpu Still Not Released

Arrest Was Carried Out Under Orders from Nanchang

He Zireng Still Related to Mitsui & Co.

He Fangpu, former compradore of Mitsui & Co., was arrested by the Zhejiang Special Task Force upon returning to his hometown of Xieqiao, Haining, and taken to the Hangzhou Provincial Public Security Bureau for questioning. The Shanghai Municipal General Assembly, the Haichang Guild, and other organizations have requested his release due to their professional and hometown connections, but he has not yet been released. It is reported that the Zhejiang authorities carried out the arrest under orders from Nanchang, indicating a very serious situation. He was arrested just two hours after returning to Xieqiao. After being taken to Hangzhou, he was interrogated twice. He admitted to having worked for Mitsui but claimed to have left the company. However, investigations revealed that although He no longer has a direct employer-employee relationship with Mitsui, his former position is now held by his eldest son, so it cannot be said that there is absolutely no connection. Furthermore, He reportedly took the opportunity to purchase Japanese sugar in bulk with each shipment, earning substantial profits. Therefore, his release will not be easy. It is also heard that party officials in Haining, upon learning of He's arrest, have requested strict punishment, considering He to be a treacherous merchant.

Reader's Advisor

On the Question of How to Read Books

| Reply to Mr. Wen from Yangzhou |

Answer: I have read your letter and the draft reading plan carefully. Based on my limited knowledge, I would like to offer my humble opinions on both the letter and the plan, hoping they may be of some use to you.

(1) Regarding your letter: You mentioned, "My studies in politics and economics are based on past learning, but during my university years, I lacked a proper method of reading, so despite years of diligent study, my gains were superficial." While this may be your modest assessment, it also reflects a general truth. However, our criticism of current university education goes beyond this. In our view, university students today suffer not just from "lacking a proper method of reading" or "superficiality." Because university education is fundamentally aimed at teaching students the path to pursuing advanced knowledge, that is, the so-called method, rather than simply providing answers. As for "superficiality," it is not a major problem for university students. In reality, universities in so-called civilized countries primarily teach officially sanctioned science, especially social science, which is often merely a defense of the interests of a few and cannot satisfy our pursuit of truth. One cannot find many economists or sociologists in universities in Europe, America, or Japan who truly fight for the majority of the people. If you are going to study in Japan for convenience of reference, it's a good plan, but if you want to study politics and economics at a university there, it's really not necessary. That's one point. In our opinion, to study politics and economics, if you have the necessary background, you can simply buy more reference books in China and that would be enough. Moreover, the study of politics and economics must be done in the daily struggles of social life and political life, not something that can be bought by spending a lot of tuition abroad. Even if you could buy it, it would be a "silver-like wax spearhead." That's the second point. So now, we want to ask you to consider:

(1) Why do you want to study politics and economics?

(2) For whose benefit are you studying politics and economics?

If you say you are pursuing knowledge for the sake of knowledge, or seeking knowledge to fill your own emptiness, then that is deceitful talk. If you say you are studying politics and economics to solve the problems of China and even the world, then you must first decide whether your research is based on the interests of individuals or a few. Once this is decided, your perspective will naturally be extremely clear, and your research methods and materials, even your observations of the same phenomena and materials, will be extraordinarily different. That's the third point.

(2) Regarding your draft reading plan: Now, no matter what science you study, foreign languages are very important. Without preparation in at least two foreign languages, you can't even be considered a researcher. Your plan to improve your foreign languages is correct. That's the first point. The subjects listed in the first stage should all be studied, so there is naturally no problem. The only question is which school of economics, political science, sociology, etc., you will base your research on... or whether you will study all schools and then settle on one. For example, when it comes to principles of economics, there are capitalist principles of economics and socialist principles of economics, and within socialism, there is a distinction between utopian socialist economics and scientific socialist economics. If you are not careful about these paths and start down the wrong road, you will be wrong from then on. That's the second point. In our opinion, the second stage should be as follows:

Second Stage: General Study of Specialized Problems:

(1) The Relationship between Economic Systems and Social Organizations;

(2) The Relationship between Rural Economy and Rural Society;

(3) The Relationship between Land Issues, Tax Policies, and Class;

(4) The Relationship between Population Issues and Production Relations, Productivity, and Production Methods;

(5) The Relationship between International Economics and Weak Nations;

(6) The Relationship between Labor Issues and Factory Management;

(7) The Relationship between Local Governments and Municipal Issues;

The so-called "system" is the written expression of an organization, and the so-called "economic system" is the written expression of an "economic organization." Studying the economic system is studying its organization; the object is one, not two. However, when we say study the relationship between the economic system and social organizations, the meaning is completely different, and at the same time, in terms of academic study, there is a scientific and historical connection. Also, while the population problem is related to the food problem, the laws of this population problem are not constant from ancient times to the present, but each era has its own special population laws. As for the current population problem (in capitalist and socialist societies), it is more closely related to "production relations, productivity, and production methods" than to food. As for the issue of "local autonomy," in reality, it is the issue of local government, that is, which group of people leads this local autonomy, and consequently, municipal issues will also be different. We believe the third stage should be: Central Study of Specialized Problems:

(1) The Relationship between China's Population Problem and International Economic Problems (the economy of imperialism and the economy of socialism).

(2) The Prospects and Inevitable Fate of Solving China's Population Problem and the Rationalization of its Economic Organization.

(3) The Aufhebung of the Opposition between City and Countryside. The term Aufhebung means eliminating their opposition and fusing their strengths into one. Some translate it as "sublation" or "annihilation," but we think a transliteration is better.

(4) The Fundamental Solution to China's Land Problem. (Since there is already item (1) in the previous section, there is no need to talk about rural construction again, because the opposition between rural and urban areas will be eliminated in the future.)

If this kind of reading plan can be implemented, then whether you are sightseeing in various parts of Japan, giving research reports, or translating or introducing famous works, it will all be possible. As for the three things to pay attention to during your three years in Japan, they are certainly important, but we believe "C" should be the first item, because only after deeply understanding the economic, political, and social situation of Japan can you truly recognize the Japanese people and their national character, and can you recognize the reasons for the success of the Meiji Restoration. As for seeking a "rational solution to the China-Japan problem," you must have a clear understanding of world history and the international situation, as well as the complex relationship between class and nation. Simply observing Japan will not find this rational solution, and even thinking only from the perspective of China itself, or even only from the interests of a few, will not find this solution.

Travel to India, Soviet Russia, and Denmark is necessary, but we want to ask why you only want to investigate India? Why only investigate Denmark? Shouldn't the United States be investigated? Shouldn't Hitler's Germany be investigated? Shouldn't Annam be investigated? As for your "specialized writings and publications" upon your return from studying abroad, of course, we who yearn to solve social problems eagerly wish for their early arrival. However, we have one request: please don't give us, these hopelessly weak "A Dou"s, any more "Shangri-La" fantasies, and don't use the illusions played by a few foreigners to preach "love for the countryside" or "urban hypocrisy" to us, these "near-death hearts that cannot be revived" weaklings! This is what we hope for from you! "Do not tell outsiders!"
