A Bird's-Eye View of Medicine and Pharmacy in Shanghai in the Last Decade (Continued)

—Pang Jingzhou

Chapter 4: The Situation of Business

The business of traditional doctors and traditional Chinese medicine merchants. From a general and sweeping perspective. People assume that it will be crowded out by new medicine. And fall into a state of decline. However, in Shanghai in the last ten years. It can be said that the business of traditional medicine and drugs is in its heyday. Why is that? Because the new trends are surging fiercely. Invisibly aroused the struggle of traditional medicine and drugs. The result of the struggle. On the contrary, there is a temporary vigorous phenomenon. But business only cares about being prosperous. And the theory does not restore the ancient times. Just look at many old doctors. Full of new terms. Such as the words "meningitis." and "cystitis". Holding a thermometer in his hand. What "high three points and drop four points" are studied. Nat. Cacodylate is prepared in the diagnosis to give people some shots. When encountering an acute illness. Be sure to ask the patient to invite a Western doctor to give a shot to strengthen the heart. Or use the efficacy of serum. While maintaining the reputation of the ancestral throat department. Even opened a Chinese medicine hospital. To move people's attention. All of this. Which one is not an ancient innovation. A blatant expression of struggle. Fortunately, the social people are a little hesitant. Using the old method. It seems that there is no enjoyment of modern civilization. Use a brand-new method. And I have never had such courage. So there is a need for this struggling-style contemporary doctor. And the contemporary doctor's business is naturally developed. Therefore, some people say 丨The prosperity of traditional medicine and drugs today. It is a fluctuating prosperity. The market is a prosperity of non-adherence. The above-mentioned several actions. Fully show the use of thermometers. The occurrence of new disease types. The efficacy of strengthening heart needles and diphtheria serum. They have all silently recognized it as accurate. But I just don’t want to praise it. This struggle will eventually be assimilated. But it’s an excellent phenomenon. correct. In the past, Japan changed from traditional Chinese medicine to scientific medicine. There is also this transitional stage. However, their government orders are good. Under a unified medical system. Even if you refer to the old method. The government only regards you as new. Therefore, Japanese medicine has. Today, there is such a day. It's ridiculous that we Chinese. But play what the National Medical Center is. I am afraid that its academic system will be chaotic. In fact, traditional doctors have two very different expectations for the National Medical Center. There is a most conservative old doctor. Of course, I hope to study ancient methods. Preserve the quintessence of the country. (This old doctor has been practicing medicine and still follows the old methods and will never be wrong.) And most of the old doctors. And the big guys who seem only semi-knowledgeable. I don’t want to refer to the new method. Specialize in making transitional doctors. To adapt to a transitional society. The mentality of this kind of person. Simply hoping that everything in China. Always wandering in the middle. But not crossing. result. The most conservative old school. Was used by this group for a while. And it was still crowded out.

Between Guangxu and Xuantong in the former Qing Dynasty. New schools were booming everywhere. A group of elderly people. With ridiculous eyes. I am afraid that no one will be able to write calligraphy, poetry, and ancient prose in the future. So I opened several ancient schools. Now those ancient schools. Has not existed for many years. However, in the past twenty years, poetry, lyrics, and songs. Although not enough to establish a country. There is no complete silence. And those who are capable are from ancient schools. The oldest faction of the National Medical Center. Looking at this example. You can also realize it.

Mr. Yu Ziwei's Will for Anatomical Dissection, A Respectful Announcement to the Public (Part 1)

— Written by Yun Xiu

Pathological anatomy is one of the most important aspects of medical science. Without it, practical medicine cannot advance. For example, the disease commonly called "stroke" in our country is understood as cerebral hemorrhage thanks to the practice of dissection in Western countries. Not only doctors but even laymen know this because they have seen and heard so much about pathological dissections of strokes. If not for this work, we would probably still be hearing from our esteemed Chinese doctors about "external strokes," "internal strokes," strokes affecting "meridians," "collaterals," "viscera," and "fu organs," with the causes attributed to "fire," "qi," or "dampness," leading to a cacophony of theories and confusion, leaving everyone bewildered. This is because they have not seen the actual pathological picture of stroke through dissection, so they just talk nonsense without anyone questioning them. Furthermore, the general public has never heard of pathological anatomy or seen the actual pathological picture of stroke as cerebral hemorrhage, so these doctors can easily deceive them with their ghost stories. This is a clear and obvious fact.

Cholera, a contagious disease, is not the same as the "wet cholera" that old Chinese doctors before the Daoguang era of the Qing dynasty described as "killing few people." It was Koch who discovered it in Egypt while studying the disease. He performed pathological dissections on cholera patients and discovered changes in the intestines, including comma-shaped bacteria in the small intestine. Later, he went to other places where cholera was rampant and performed pathological dissections on many cholera corpses to confirm that the comma-shaped bacteria were indeed the pathogens of epidemic cholera. Now,

we use these comma-shaped bacteria to create a solution for preventive injections, and its effectiveness has been recognized worldwide. Last year, cholera was raging fiercely, but Shanghai had relatively few cases and deaths. This is due to the strict implementation of preventive injections. The comma-shaped bacteria solution has saved countless lives, as numerous as the sands of the Ganges. If the Egyptians had not been willing to sacrifice their corpses, Koch would not have been able to perform so many pathological dissections, and he might not have discovered the comma-shaped bacteria or confirmed that they were the pathogens of cholera. Then, of course, there would be no preventive injection and no proactive epidemic prevention work. To this day, we might still be relying on Taoist rituals and deity worship as preventive measures. This is another clear and obvious fact.

From the first fact, we can understand that without pathological anatomy, we will never understand the true nature of diseases. Before pathological anatomy was practiced, people around the world who died from illnesses had no idea what had killed them, truly "dying without knowing why!" Let me give you two examples. The first is Mr. Xu, a wealthy merchant from Ningbo. Mr. Xu suffered from a stomach ailment, and I was called to examine him. His symptoms were frequent vomiting, stomach pain, and the vomited stomach contents had a sour taste, often with blood, resembling coffee grounds, and with abnormal fermentation and putrid odor. I diagnosed stomach cancer, but many other doctors said it was not cancer. Their reason was that there was hydrochloric acid in the stomach, and his skin color was not very pale (cachexia). Later, X-rays showed that the stomach was smooth and round, without any unevenness. The X-ray specialist said, "Definitely not stomach cancer." I saw the X-ray picture of the stomach and found it strange, but I couldn't see anything below the pylorus, so I said, "We still can't rely on the area below the pylorus." But I was also suspicious, perhaps my diagnosis was wrong. Later, the pyloric stenosis became more severe, completely blocked. I had no choice but to consult renowned foreign surgical experts for surgery. Who knew that upon opening the abdomen, almost all of the intestinal tract below the pylorus was cancerous, making it impossible to operate. He died a few days later. When I heard the news, I finally understood. Mr. Xu's cancer was not in the stomach, so the stomach X-ray was smooth and without bumps, and the secretion of hydrochloric acid was not completely absent. As for the lack of cachexia, it was because Mr. Xu was well-cared for, and cachexia is not the only evidence for cancer diagnosis. Later, on the day of the funeral, I went to pay my respects. Mr. Xu's eldest son asked me, "If we hadn't had surgery, wouldn't he have died so quickly?" I said, "According to the diagnosis after the surgery, it was indeed cancer and had spread beyond control. Your father's condition was hopeless. Even without surgery, it would only have prolonged his suffering for twenty or thirty days. What good would that do? In my opinion, it was fortunate that he had surgery. Now we know that there was no hope for your father's illness, and you have done your best as a son. We understand the nature of the illness thoroughly. Otherwise, after he died, there would still be many doubts and regrets, thinking that some method might have saved him, or that some other doctor might have been better. And we doctors would still be puzzled about whether it was cancer or not. Now we have solid evidence, and doubts can be dispelled. Not only does the deceased know that his fate was sealed, but his children and friends also understand that it was an incurable disease, which can reduce some of the sorrow." I said these words, and Mr. Xu's eldest son nodded, seeming to accept them. In fact, my words were the truth. How many of our countrymen die without knowing why! After they die, there is still much discussion and blame. The unfortunate doctors are criticized by the family for the medicine being too hot or the prescription too aggressive, or the needle too sharp, causing endless disputes and confusion. Once the coffin is sealed and buried, this injustice will never be redressed. In our country, I encounter these cases not just in a year, but in a month, in a day. Without solid evidence to show them, the doctors who made the wrong diagnosis will never know their mistake, and no one will prove the accuracy of the doctors who made the right diagnosis. No wonder the doctors call out "fire," "dampness," "spirit," and "phlegm" randomly, and the old women talk nonsense about "ghosts," "gods," "foxes," and "wild cats." Because there is no thorough investigation, there is chaos. In Mr. Xu's case, I feel that the doctors who examined him learned many valuable lessons. Even my initial thought that it was cancer almost wavered and I couldn't hold my ground. I also learned a lot and am very grateful. (To be continued)

Suggestions for Collecting "Sanitary Fines"

— Song Guobin

▲▲…………▲▲

It is said, "The people can be made to follow a path, but they cannot be made to understand it." This is because among the common people, there are both good and bad, with differences in knowledge and variations in morality. Fathers and sons are not the same, and husbands and wives are not equal. The establishment of laws is to remedy the shortcomings of etiquette and education. The masses of the people lack education and only know their own interests. They do not care about committing wrongdoing or breaking the law. They regard public rules as unimportant. If there is no legal restraint, they will become increasingly reckless and not know where to stop. "Guiding them with virtue" is not as effective as "disciplining them with punishment." Although this is criticized by ancient Confucian scholars as deviating from the path of kings and condemned by modern scholars as undermining civil rights, I believe that when the people's intelligence is not fully developed and education is not widespread, when the boundaries of rights and the scope of freedom are not clear, the words of the Legalists cannot be completely abandoned. Excess and deficiency both deviate from the golden mean. Laws are meant to protect the freedom of the people, and their effectiveness depends on the way they are used. Based on this principle, regarding sanitation, my suggestions are as follows:

China's attention to sanitation administration has been lacking for a long time. Since the national government established its capital, it has gradually become aware of this and has set up departments in the central government and bureaus in various cities to manage it. However, after several years, the results have not been obvious. When discussing sanitation, one cannot help but sigh deeply. The level of sanitation knowledge among the people is also extremely low. Although doctors like us are involved in this, newspapers have medical supplements, and magazines have specialized

Page 12

articles, we have used up our pens and ink in writing and exhausted our mouths and tongues in persuading, but the speakers are earnest and the listeners are indifferent. These two achievements make us blush with shame! Examining the wise teachings of the past and verifying them with the current facts, we know that the foolish people cannot be reasoned with, and that good laws do not harm the harmony of nature. Empty words are of no use, and effective results are difficult to achieve. Legal sanctions are probably the only effective method. I briefly list three measures for the authorities to consider:

(1) Promulgate various sanitation laws, ordering all institutions, shops, factories, and families throughout the country to abide by them.

(2) Train high-level sanitation inspectors and assign them to various regions. Their duties are as follows:

(1) Inspecting the sanitation of households.

(2) Investigating school sanitation.

(3) Investigating the sanitation facilities and conditions of various institutions (such as prisons, factories, and hospitals).

(4) Examining prostitutes.

(5) Inspecting the sanitation of ships and trains.

(3) Train a number of sanitation police in each city or county and assign them to various districts. Their duties are as follows:

(1) Inspecting slaughterhouses and food stores to see if there are any violations of sanitation regulations.

(2) Inspecting the locations of garbage and excrement to see if they comply with sanitation laws.

(3) Inspecting the sanitation of hotels.

(4) Inspecting bathhouses and barbershops.

(5) Inspecting pedestrians to see if they spit or defecate in public places.

The above are just examples, and I know I am omitting many things. However, in all things in the world, there are advantages and disadvantages. There are no unchanging rules from ancient to modern times, and there are no perfect laws. Training sanitation personnel can be effective in the short term, but the matter involves changes in scope. How can we avoid corruption? The corruption leads to blatant extortion, harming good people. Private bribery conceals wrongdoing. Is this harming the people in the name of benefiting them? The way to remedy this cannot be delayed. To summarize, there are three items:

(1) Promote moral education to train their character.

(2) Allow accusations to expose their conspiracies.

(3) Organize a supervisory team to monitor their actions.

The procedure for punishing unsanitary conditions is generally carried out in two parts. Those who violate sanitation laws are first persuaded or warned. If they do not listen, they are fined to serve as a warning. The proceeds from the fines are used for sanitation construction and not for other purposes. Imposing penalties while collecting revenue is beneficial to the country and the people. Isn't this killing two birds with one stone? It depends on the actual practice of our sanitation authorities.

Preface to "Sexual Medicine" by Scholar Qing

— Wang Qizhang

The structure of the world and the reproduction of living things all originate from sex, and all originate from desire. Mencius, when speaking of human nature, first mentioned food and sex. However, food and sex are a mixture of sexual and other desires, not purely sexual. Sex is individual, differing according to species, while desire is common, differing only in degree. Speaking of sex, satisfying hunger is the nature of birds, adapting to pasture is the nature of horses, swimming well is the nature of pigs, being difficult to tame is the nature of dragons, escaping cold and seeking warmth is the nature of fish, and never leaving the forest is the nature of bustards. The nature of things is inherently different, but none can be without the desire for beauty. Although humans are intelligent, how can they escape this? Even the Buddha, who is said to be pure in the six senses and to be neither born nor destroyed, seems to have no sex or desire. Lao Tzu and Zhuang Tzu, who advocated non-action, also seem to have no sex or desire. However, the eight generations of Buddha, Lao Tzu, and Zhuang Tzu could not avoid sex and desire. In the world, it is difficult to go against sex and desire. How can we expect the masses to transcend and be unique? Therefore, sex and desire come with all things, like the soul inseparable from the body. Many people have discussed sex in the past, but unfortunately, they were half-bound by etiquette and half-confined by speculation. If they touched on male and female sexual desire, they avoided speaking about it. It is said that Zhang Bi refused to answer the emperor's questions about bedroom matters, considering them obscene and unfit for the court. Even the sages and the wise were said to have married late after acquiring knowledge, which was considered impossible in the world but was recorded in the classics and passed down through the ages, becoming a beautiful story. Thus, for thousands of years, human nature has not been extinguished, flourishing in secret, and reproduction has been abundant in secret, without knowing why. Now, with the progress of science, the excavation of life, the survival of the fittest, and the rectification of bloodlines, the theories of strengthening the race and eugenics have arisen together. Scholars, seeking the source and exploring the root, have focused on the innate problem of reproduction. Therefore, to improve the race, we must first study the structure and organs of reproduction and the pathways of sexual desire, so that people can follow the rules, young people can avoid wrong paths, and those who fall into traps can know how to extricate themselves. Leaders can teach future generations. Therefore, in various countries, the departments of urology and reproduction have now become independent. However, our old moral standards still exist, and society avoids talking about it. To this day, there is still a lack of complete and specialized books. There are only a few fragmented chapters and remnants, which are not works that hit the mark. Scholar Qian Yiqing has broken his arm in this field for many years and has used his great writing skills to create this beautiful and specialized book. It first describes the structure of the reproductive organs, then the physiology and hygiene of sexual desire, and then the treatment of various diseases of the reproductive organs, concluding with eugenics. From this, we know that the author's purpose is upright and bright. However, today, the issue of eugenics is just beginning and has not yet reached the stage of practical implementation. However, informed people believe that we do not need to personally experience success to hold a sincere wish. We deeply hope that people in society and colleagues in the field will read it with the same method as reading the three hundred poems of the Book of Songs. Then Mr. Qian's work will not be in vain.

Recent Preventive Medicine

— Yin Ge

Calmette and the successful simultaneous immunization against diphtheria. There is the tuberculosis immunization invented by Professor Calmette. He also researched it at the Pasteur Institute. For example, typhoid and cholera bacteria can be killed with chemicals (i.e., placing the bacteria in a chemical solution) to create a bacterial suspension. Injecting this liquid under the skin can achieve a certain degree of immunity for preventive purposes. However, tuberculosis bacteria are different. A suspension of dead bacteria cannot be used for immunization. Therefore, the medical community believed that only live tuberculosis bacteria could be used for tuberculosis immunization. However, after many failures, everyone agreed that harmless live tuberculosis bacteria could not be found. Since Koch discovered tuberculosis bacteria, there have been no findings for fifty years. Until recently, the old professor Calmette and his student Gralla, both at the Pasteur Institute in Paris, collaborated and used a special culture medium designed by Calmette to repeatedly culture highly virulent tuberculosis bacteria. Later, the hereditary physicochemical structure of the tuberculosis bacteria changed. Calmette worked tirelessly on the culture for thirteen years, oblivious to everything else. In Europe, his homeland was in danger, and the sound of cannons could be heard far and wide. However, Calmette continued to culture bacteria and conduct research at the Pasteur Institute. Finally, he obtained tuberculosis bacteria that were non-toxic to animals and definitively proved that a special immunity to tuberculosis bacteria could be created in the animal body. This is like domesticating wild animals. After hundreds of generations, the animals lose their wild nature, become harmless to humans, and become livestock. The tuberculosis bacteria cultured by Calmette are like these harmless livestock.

Calmette and his student Gralla worked hard together and finally succeeded. Therefore, the bacteria were named Calmette-Gralla bacteria in their memory. The abbreviation in Western languages is BCG. B stands for bacteria, C for Calmette, and G for Gralla.

His experiments were very meticulous. The order was to first test on calves, then monkeys, rabbits, rats, etc., and finally humanoid apes. The scope of his research was extensive, and his intentions were very thorough. In 1922, Dr. Huerle, a pediatrician at the Paris Medical University, first tested it on newborns and confirmed that it was harmless and effective. When his experimental report was published, French women competed to have their children vaccinated. From 1924 to 1930, a total of 200,000 infants were vaccinated, and the infant mortality rate was greatly reduced.

This vaccination method is extremely simple. Within ten days of the infant's birth, three packets of medicine are used. Every two days, the medicine is placed in a small spoon to create two cc of BCG suspension. Thirty minutes before breastfeeding, when the stomach is empty, it is mixed with breast milk and given to the infant. This suspension has no odor, and the child can drink it without realizing it. It does not harm the stomach or intestines, and it does not cause fever. It is the same as drinking milk. Why can immunization be achieved without injection? Because the intestines of infants are the same as the intestines of young animals. The ability to pass bacteria and antitoxins is very strong. After drinking the BCG suspension, the bacteria pass through the intestinal wall and enter the infant's lymphatic vessels, circulating throughout the body and creating tuberculosis immunization. According to recent research, BCG should be vaccinated again at the end of the first year and at the end of the third year. The effectiveness is more certain. However, at this time, the intestinal wall is not as able to pass bacteria as it is in newborns, so a subcutaneous injection is used instead.

Smallpox has epidemic periods, but tuberculosis has the opportunity to infect at any time. It can be said to be in an epidemic period all year round. Infants have the opportunity to be infected from birth, so prevention is necessary. As for older children or adults, subcutaneous injections can be given to prevent the spread of tuberculosis.

In France, you can buy the vaccine from the Pasteur Institute in Paris by telegram or mail. The institute sends it immediately upon receiving the letter. The mother usually mixes it with breast milk on the third, fifth, seventh, or sixth, eighth day after the child is born and has the infant drink it. The method is simple, and mothers are very happy. Calmette has also received the highest medal from the French government and is extremely honored.

(Editor's note) Pulmonary tuberculosis is a major enemy of mankind. Since the discovery of tuberculosis bacteria, the whole world has paid attention to its immunization methods, but very few have been effective. BCG is one of them. This method has been very effective in France, Belgium, Italy, etc. However, there are no detailed reports in the UK, Germany, and the United States. Presumably, it is still under study. Yin Ge's article introduces the latest theories in extremely simple language and is published in a special edition. We hope readers will pay attention.

Scientific Ways to Preserve Life (19)

— Yu Songyun

(15) Management of the External Genitalia

(A) Consequences of Uncleanliness

After childbirth, the external genitalia of the postpartum woman become the source of lochia, mucus, blood, and other discharges. Therefore, the external genitalia, lower limbs, waist, and abdomen are inevitably soiled and difficult to clean. Even the bed linens and clothes are soiled. If one is not careful, it is easy to be attacked by fungi and dangerous changes can occur.

The most important consequence of uncleanliness of the external genitalia is the cause of puerperal fever. Although there are various causes of puerperal fever, the starting point is of course from uncleanliness and susceptibility to bacterial toxins. For example, the fingers of the midwife who delivers the baby are not disinfected, or the fingers of the doctor or midwife are not sufficiently disinfected. During childbirth, the midwife uses soiled instruments and makes unreasonable incisions, or the medical instruments or cotton swabs are not completely disinfected. The lochia does not stop and accumulates in the genitals. Then, the fungus directly invades the uterus. Before long, the onset of puerperal fever is announced.

In the past, people only knew that it was easier to get sick after childbirth than before pregnancy. Even if the postpartum woman delivered by a midwife was fortunate enough not to be cut during labor, many still died of illness after childbirth. This was because they did not fully understand the cause of puerperal fever, so they arbitrarily managed the external genitalia and recklessly ignored it. When danger occurred, they still did not understand the origin of this danger. Isn't that a joke? In this era, it is not difficult to understand this cause. Then, one should pay full attention to the external genitalia after childbirth and add thorough prevention to be happy.

(B) Cleaning the External Genitalia

The external genitalia and the surrounding area should be washed with sterilized warm water and a soft cloth or cotton swabs from the beginning of delivery. Then, sterilize with 2% carbolic acid water or 1% Lysol solution. Wash and wipe it directly from time to time during the delivery process. It is also necessary to wash and wipe this within a week after delivery. If there is a wound, you can sprinkle it with Dematoffin, etc., and then cover the external genitalia with sterilized cotton gauze. However, vaginal irrigation must be guided by a doctor or midwife. If there are no abnormal symptoms after delivery, there is no need for vaginal irrigation.

(C) Lacerations of the External Genitalia

During childbirth, the fetus passes through the vulva, and at the same time, abdominal pressure increases. The baby's head emerges naturally. If pathological changes occur, leading to prolonged labor or the baby's head being delayed, the external genitalia will be lacerated. Also, if it is a first-time mother of advanced age, the soft birth canal may become hardened. This is also a cause of lacerations of the external genitalia. If it has been lacerated, it should be disinfected immediately with minimal strength and a doctor should be requested quickly. Sutures should be performed at the site of the laceration.

Scientific Studies on Cleanliness

— Guo Renji

Our lives proceed accompanied by uncleanliness, because the human body is a manufacturing plant for uncleanliness. With every breath, we pollute the atmosphere. In an instant, our shirts become soiled. No matter how noble our lives, no one can suppress the excretion of feces and urine for even a day. Even the noses of beautiful women have mucus, ears have earwax, eyes have eye discharge, and mouths have dental plaque. We often criticize pigs for living in filth, but how can our lives surpass theirs? Our living places are also dirtied by our lives. However, we can remove the uncleanliness in our leisure time. This is the point of human superiority. If we do not care about uncleanliness at all, we are barely superior to pigs. The unclean things we produce are of no benefit to the human body. They are not only unnecessary, but they also increase unpleasantness in life, are disliked by others, and are very harmful. Therefore, we must strive to eliminate uncleanliness and must study and seek a proper method of cleanliness for the sake of the joy and beauty of life.

Sensory Uncleanliness Generally, when we drink water and find a grain of rice in it, we feel that the water is unclean. But in reality, is it directly harmful? Some people are so clean that they do not go to the toilet unless they are naked, and they do not pick up chopsticks unless they wash their hands three times. This is because their senses are more acute than ordinary people. Their nerves are not physiological, but pathological. We call it mysophobia. This is not a good example. The harm of mysophobia is not much different from the harm of non-mysophobia. Why is it beneficial to seek cleanliness beyond what is necessary, and to neglect important cleanliness? It is not uncommon for things that do not feel unclean to be very unclean and dangerous. It is dangerous to judge cleanliness based solely on the five senses. This is why there is a need for research on the left. (To be continued)

Education News

Important News

Ministry of Education Order

Three Universities to Suspend Enrollment of Political Science Students

Based on the Central Education Reform Plan and the merger of liberal arts and law colleges, the Ministry of Education has ordered universities to suspend the enrollment of new students in the following departments for the next academic year: the Department of Politics and the Department of Sociology at Bian University, the Department of Politics at Zhejiang University, and the Department of Politics at Hebei Provincial College of Law and Commerce. Existing students in these departments will be allowed to graduate, after which the departments will be abolished.

Cheng Qibao and Others Return to Beijing After Meeting Chiang

Statement by Mr. Cheng Regarding the Alumni Association of Jinan University

Five education commissioners, including Cheng Qibao, who were on a fact-finding trip to Europe, recently met with Chiang in Jiangxi and Shanxi provinces at his invitation. They returned to Beijing yesterday from Jiangxi. When interviewed by reporters at the Ministry of Education, in addition to inquiring about the details of the trip, Mr. Cheng also addressed the matter of the open letter from the Jinan University Alumni Association published in the newspapers. He stated that the content of the letter was completely inconsistent with the facts. He explained that when he and his colleagues (Cheng referring to himself) passed through Singapore, he had discussed overseas Chinese education at a welcome reception for overseas Chinese, which was well received by the overseas Chinese present. Regarding Jinan University, he only hoped for its continued development and the completion of its mission, and had absolutely no intention of slandering it. The Ministry of Education's various measures and reform plans are the responsibility of the administrative head, and have nothing to do with Cheng Qibao. In conclusion, he acknowledged that the Alumni Association's intention to protect their alma mater was admirable. If the association wished to discuss overseas Chinese education based on research and careful analysis, he was willing to participate from an educational standpoint. However, if they disregarded the facts and made reckless attacks, which would not help the situation, then he would not accept their invitation.

Local News

University Education Association of Shanghai Invited Zhang Taiyan to Lecture on Cultural Revival Yesterday

Historically Presented Evidence Proving Manchuria is Chinese Territory

Conclusion: To Save the Nation, One Must First Study History

The University Faculty Association of Shanghai invited the renowned scholar Zhang Taiyan to give a second academic lecture yesterday. Over five hundred members of the association, including Zhang Shouyong, Kang Xuanyi, Lin Zhongke, Wu Zijing, Jiang Liangfu, Ouyang Xi, Chen Jilie, as well as teachers and students from various schools, attended the lecture. Zhang Shouyong presided over the meeting, Chen Jilie served as the master of ceremonies, and after the customary greetings, Mr. Zhang began his lecture. The gist of his speech was that national history is like an individual's account book. If an individual forgets their account book, their real estate may be encroached upon without their knowledge. If a nation is ignorant of its history, its territory may be lost without remorse. Therefore, those who seek to destroy a nation always start by destroying its history. When Qin conquered the six states, it burned the books of the six states. When Japan sought to subjugate Korea, it first destroyed Korean history. History is the root of all culture, like the skin to fur. If the skin is gone, where will the fur attach? Mr. Zhang cited various historical evidences to prove that Manchuria, Chahar, and Rehe were all part of Chinese territory. He also cited precise statistics to show that Manchus actually constituted a minority in the Northeast. There was absolutely no reason to allow them to use the pretext of national self-determination to establish an independent state. It was not surprising that the Japanese distorted the facts, but it was lamentable that most Chinese people were ignorant of their own history and unfamiliar with the evolution of their own national territory, which was like Zhang Zongchang not knowing the number of his own concubines. Therefore, to arouse national consciousness and revive Chinese culture, one must study history. Even the success of the Xinhai Revolution was largely due to the inspiration derived from historical studies. Finally, Chairman Zhang Shouyong elaborated further on Zhang's ideas and then announced the adjournment of the meeting.

Awards Ceremony for Children's Music Broadcasting Competition

The awards ceremony for the All-Shanghai Children's Broadcasting Competition, jointly organized by the Shanghai Children's Morning Post, the Yong Sheng and Heng Sen Radio Stations, the China National Goods Company, and the Shanghai Lili Company, was held at 2:00 PM yesterday on the second floor of the China National Goods Company on Nanjing Road. Mayor Wu (represented by Director Pan), Director Pan of the Municipal Education Bureau, and judges Yan Duhe, Xu Zhuodai, Ding Song, Hu Shuyi, as well as guests Yao Mulian, Dan Duyu, Gu Wuwei, and others attended. Sports

Track and Field Competition: Baihong Team Overwhelms Russian Émigrés

Motovkin Breaks Chinese 16-Pound Shot Put Record with 12.74 Meters

Chen Baoqiu Second with 12.08 Meters

Score: 53 to 29

The Baihong Track and Field Team overwhelmed the strong Russian Émigré Sports Association with a score of 53 to 29, winning the silver cup presented by Director Pan Gongzhan of the Education Bureau. Team captain Cheng Yize of the renowned team hosted a banquet at the Daya Restaurant last night to celebrate the victory.

Outstanding Performance: The most outstanding performance was undoubtedly Motovkin's 16-pound shot put, breaking Liu Renxiu's national record of 12.24 meters with a throw of 12.74 meters. Although Chen Baoqiu came in second, his score of 12.08 meters was also commendable. Motovkin also broke the Chinese 12-pound shot put record at the Five-Group Sports Meet with a throw of over 45 feet. This person is assured of first place in the All-China Games. Secondly, Zeng Rongzhong's 400 meters in 54 seconds was also a good performance, surpassing Guan Changfa. Qiqiliefu's 10,000 meters in exactly 36 minutes was crisp and clean, leaving Chen Xuzhou behind by 400 meters. Other achievements included Wang Yongmin's triple jump of 13.2 meters and Jiemujin's high jump of 1.77 meters, all above average. The Russian Émigré team's defeat was due to their small number of participants, with only one person competing in the hurdles and 400 meters, and the 200 meters being cancelled due to the Russian Émigrés' lack of personnel. Second Day of Zhejiang Provincial Games

Fourteen New Records Set in Two Days

Track and Field Concludes Today, Ball Games Begin Tomorrow

(Hangzhou, 28th) The Zhejiang Provincial Games opened in Hangzhou on the first day (27th). The weather was unfavorable, affecting the progress of the competition. Around 4:00 PM, heavy rain poured down, ending the competition. Events that could not be held on the first day included the high jump (already held for the college group), the 400-meter intermediate hurdles, the triple jump, the 1500 meters, and the men's junior 200-meter intermediate hurdles. The rain did not stop the night before. Although the rain stopped yesterday morning, the sky was overcast with occasional light rain. The program was heavy, and the competition had to continue. It started at 9:00 AM. The venue was very wet, making it inconvenient to throw heavy objects, but this had no impact on the track events. There were few participants, and not many schools or groups visited. The weather was quite good in the afternoon, with sunshine. The number of spectators increased sharply, and the referees worked hard, without rest, to ensure that the heavy schedule could be completed on time. Ball games will begin tomorrow.

Yesterday's Finals

College Group Intermediate Hurdles This event continued from the first day. There were no preliminary rounds, and the final began directly. Aviation's Jin Huaizhi took the lead, with a steady attitude and excellent hurdle technique, wasting no time, and achieved a good result of 61.2 seconds, setting a new Zhejiang provincial record. He won easily, leading by twenty yards. Zhijiang's Zhu Kaiyuan was second, and Zhijiang's Hu Mingren was third, barely making it to the finish line.

Public Group High Jump This also continued from the first day. Linhai's Yu Guangzhao won the championship with 1.62 meters, which was considered a good result in an average competition. Fenghua's Dai Licheng was second with 1.58 meters, Hangzhou's Yan Youcang was third, and Yinxian's He Xiaoti was fourth.

Hong Yongtang Sets New 1500-Meter Record in Men's Junior Division

4 Minutes 42.6 Seconds

In the 1500-meter final, Zhijiang's Wu Zhigao finished first in the college group with a mediocre time of 5 minutes and 6 seconds. In the public group, Hangzhou's Zhao Baode broke Ling Tingquan's Zhejiang provincial record of 4 minutes and 54.6 seconds with a time of 4 minutes and 52.4 seconds. In the men's senior group, Ling Tingquan from District 1 broke his own original record and the newly created record of 4 minutes and 2 seconds by Zhao Baode with a time of 4 minutes and 45.2 seconds. However, in the men's junior group, Hong Yongtang from District 2 broke all previous and current records with a time of 4 minutes and 42.6 seconds, regaining the highest Zhejiang provincial record. This person is nimble and light-footed, and achieving this result was no accident. He is truly a promising talent.

Men's Senior High Jump Xu Huang (District 4) won first place. His form was not beautiful, and the height was 1.54 meters, far less than the public group. Qian Chengfeng from District 2 was second with 1.52 meters, a very small difference from the first place. Lin Zaiwei (District 2) was around 1.50 meters, and Chuan Jun from District 1 was fourth with 1.49 meters.

Public Group Intermediate Hurdles There were no good performances. Everyone knocked down hurdles, and by the last two hurdles, they were exhausted, barely clearing them, and their form was terrible. Hangzhou's Jin Mengjiang finished first with a very poor time of 68.2 seconds.

Men's Senior Intermediate Hurdles District 1 and District 2 split the honors, each getting two places. However, District 1 won a total of seven points. Xu Shiyan finished first with a very poor time of 67 seconds. Their form was not good, but the competition was intense.

College 1500 Meters Aviation's Le Yiqin and Zhijiang's Wu Zhigao competed fiercely. Meng Guangxin was also well-known and unwilling to be outdone. They fought for the lead, and the competition was even. In the end, Zhijiang's Wu Zhigao finished first, Le was second, and Meng was third, with a mediocre time of 5 minutes and 6 seconds.

Public 1500 Meters This final was also a continuation of yesterday's program. In this group, Hangzhou's Zhao Baode set a new Zhejiang provincial record with a time of 4 minutes and 52.4 seconds, breaking the original record of 4 minutes and 54.6 seconds held by Ling Tingquan. Jin Zhiming from Wuxing was second, Rong Shilin from Hangxian was third, and Xu Shouqiang from Tiantai was fourth.

Men's Senior 1500 Meters Ling Tingquan (District 1), who holds the highest Zhejiang provincial record for this event, was in excellent form and had a large stride. He broke his own record with a time of 4 minutes and 45.2 seconds, re-establishing the new Zhejiang provincial record and far surpassing Zhao Baode's new record in the public group. Yu Fengmao from District 2 was second, Hu Dewen from District 2 was third, and Xiao Shaopei from District 1 was fourth.

Women's Senior High Jump Zhou Xiexiang (District 1), Si Feng (District 1), and Zhou Yuru (District 1) competed fiercely. Their skills were equal. In the end, Zhou Xiexiang won the championship, Si Feng was second, and Zhou Yuru was third. Zhu Jiasun was fourth. All were from District 1. The result was 1.24 meters, which was quite good.

Men's Senior 100 Meters The semifinal for this event was cancelled, and the final was held yesterday. Chen Jiarui and Chuan Jun, the first-place winners in the two preliminary groups, had similar skills and both intended to compete for the championship. However, Li Shouzhen was also determined and exerted his energy to strive for a high position. The situation was quite tense. Chen Jiarui ultimately won first place with a time of 12.4 seconds. Chuan Jun was third, and Li Shouzhen took second. Gao Depei finished fourth.

Public 100 Meters This group also had no semifinals and held the final at the same time as the men's senior. Hangzhou's Chen Kuizhang had the best preliminary result and was very hopeful for the final. However, merit prevails, and Chen ultimately won the championship with a time of 12.5 seconds. Ge Qukang followed closely behind and took second place. Guo Qiaozhi was third, and He Kaoti was fourth.

Women's Senior 100 Meters Ju Bin had the best preliminary result, followed by Ma Yumei. The final yesterday lived up to expectations. Ju finished first and Ma finished second with a time of 15.3 seconds. Ju set a new Zhejiang provincial record, beating Rong Shuzhen's original record (15.4 seconds) by 0.1 seconds. Zheng Hanshu was third, and Zhang Zhuhua was fourth.

Group Calisthenics Performance

Yesterday at 8:30 a.m., morning exercises began. Participants included female students from four schools: Hangzhou Normal High School, Hangzhou Girls' High School, and the two departments of the Municipal High School. The whole group was unified, with a lively attitude and agile movements. Amidst the graceful movements, there was a vigorous spirit. Next was the American-style freehand exercise by the female students of Hangzhou Normal School. The performance was pure and enthusiastic, with many changes, and could be called outstanding. Following this was the imitative exercise by Muxing Middle School. At that time, the weather was not cooperating. Fine rain was drizzling, and the cold wind was blowing, making people want to leave. However, the students of Muxing School performed neatly and with full spirit, which shows that their daily training was effective. Next was the flexibility exercise by the male students of the Municipal High School. The steps were orderly and the movements were in sync. Finally, there was the flexibility exercise by the Provincial First High School. The movements were looping and reciprocating, and turning around in the middle, which was quite worth seeing. After the exercise was over, suddenly a "handkerchief passing competition" was added, the pattern was new, and the turn of the face was particularly open, which was especially unique.

Shanghai tennis veteran Carnavalo, a Portuguese national, has dominated the Shanghai tennis scene for many years. In 1923, he won the Shanghai Senior Singles Championship. Over the years, he has represented Shanghai in inter-port matches. He is a highly experienced veteran who has trained many young male and female tennis players. Carnavalo has announced that from now on, he is leaving amateur status and becoming a professional tennis player, fully dedicating himself to coaching young talents. His contact address is at the Shishi Foreign Firm on Nanjing Road.
